# Calendar Search Actions Setup - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

⌘K

Actions

Calendar Search Actions Setup

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

You can set up a Calendar Search Action in Glean to integrate calendar data with multiple Glean features, such as:

*   Search
*   Home Page
*   Agents

You can choose between two meeting ecosystems for your organization:

*   Google Calendar & Meet
*   Microsoft Outlook & Teams

When you set up a calendar search action for your organization, you are influencing the functionality of these features. How calendar data is integrated and what data is available to Glean depends on your meeting ecosystem. You can use the table below to identify supported functionality across Calendar event and a meeting Transcript elements:

| Meeting element | Search | Home page summarization | Glean Chat queries | Agent |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Microsoft Outlook Calendar events | Searching for Outlook calendar events is supported | Supported through calendar events on Calendar card on home page | Querying for past outlook events is supported | Ability to fetch Outlook calendar events through Calendar Search Action is supported |
| Microsoft Teams transcripts | Unsupported due to unavailability of transcript URL from Microsoft | Summarization of team transcripts is supported. Follow-up Q&A is unsupported | Querying for past teams transcripts is supported | Ability to fetch transcript is unsupported |
| Google Calendar events | Searching for Google calendar events is supported | Supported through calendar events on Calendar card on home page | Querying for past Google calendar events is supported | Ability to fetch Google calendar events through Calendar Search Action is supported |
| Google Meet transcript | Supported through app:googlecalendar, meeting title search and structured results (based on ranking relevance) | Summarization of Meet transcripts and follow-up Q&A is unsupported | Querying for past Google meet transcripts is supported | Google transcripts are stored as a Google doc. Ability to read transcript documents is supported |

Perform the following connector setup steps to set up the calendar search action for your meeting ecosystem:

[Google Calendar\
---------------](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/native/gcal/native-setup)
[Microsoft Teams\
---------------](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/native/teams/teams-transcripts)

To use calendar search actions as part of an Agent, refer to the [Calendar Search Action](https://docs.glean.com/agents/actions/glean/calendar-search)
 article.

General

About the Admin Console

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)

[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Key Features](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about#key-features)
    

The Glean Admin Console is a central hub within Glean that allows admins to manage and configure their deployment. It is designed to be user-friendly and self-served, empowering customer admins to set up their deployment without needing a dedicated project.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about#key-features)

Key Features
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Role Based Access Control (RBAC):** Admins can manage what permissions teammates have via the Teammates page of the Admin Console. They can grant a user permission to moderate content, or relevate them to either Full Admin or Setup Admin roles.
*   **Authentication Settings:** Admins can configure which Identity Provider (IdP) is configured for Single Sign-On (SSO).
*   **Search Management:** Admins can check whether a user has access to a document within Glean, or hide documents from appearing in search results.
*   **Datasource Management:** Admins can manage and configure the datasources that Glean can access. This includes adding new datasources, removing existing ones, and adjusting the permissions and access levels.
*   **Glean Assistant Setup:** Admins can set up Glean Assistant, which covers Generative AI features such as chat, answers, and summarization.
*   **Manage Adoption**: Admins can track the people in their company who haven’t yet been invited to Glean, who have received an invite, and who are actively using Glean - all in a single view.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/managing-your-glean-deployment/admin-features-in-glean)
.

[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

Microsoft Actions can easily be turned off if you would like to turn them off. Customers can easily do this by following these steps:

*   Go to [Glean](https://app.glean.com/admin/platform/tools)
     and navigate to Admin -> Actions,
*   From the Actions list that appears, select Microsoft Actions and go to the Microsoft Actions page
*   Then do one of the following:
    *   Either delete the whole action pack by clicking on “More” and then Delete ![Delete Action Pack](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/administration/assistant/actions/disable-microsoft-actions/10aee8117dde7e14814ff823780ec109.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=4121507c1d60b2185e677bafe841aac0)
    *   Or if you want to disable Microsoft actions from appearing in a specific surface (e.g. don’t allow Microsoft actions to trigger as follow-ups in chat responses but still allow them to be available as an export option). Follow these steps:
        *   Scroll down to Publish settings in the Microsoft Actions page.
        *   Click on Edit. ![Edit Publish Settings](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/administration/assistant/actions/disable-microsoft-actions/966366ab0f5dc68a1beaf9ef55cee69b.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=4998c65fdb35932b3fbe0be447aa62b3)
        *   Toggle off any surface they don’t want Microsoft Actions to appear in. ![Toggle Off Surfaces](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/administration/assistant/actions/disable-microsoft-actions/d8d0f9c2f56444308cb987b21712e122.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=17a64e6f80fca7891a27d7328b1f9ec8)

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/actions/how-to-turn-off-microsoft-actions)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Github Actions Setup](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/github-actions-setup)

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Action Pack setup instructions](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#action-pack-setup-instructions)

The Databricks action pack contains the following actions:

*   Search Databricks with SQL
*   Search Databricks with Genie

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#action-pack-setup-instructions)

Action Pack setup instructions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#note-on-databricks-urls-needed-for-setup)

Note on Databricks URLs needed for Setup

*   The host URL is the same URL that is used to login into Databricks instance. The formats differ for AWS, GCP, Azure, as given below:
    *   AWS: `https://<databricks-instance-id>.cloud.databricks.com/`
    *   GCP: `https://<databricks-instance-id>.gcp.databricks.com/`
    *   Azure: `https://adb-<databricks-instance-id>.<number>.azuredatabricks.net/`
*   To get the Genie Space Id- when you have the Genie Space open in the Databricks UI, you can get the Genie Space Id from the URL. `https://<databricks-instance-id>.cloud.databricks.com/genie?rooms/<genie-space-id>/o=<anothernumber>`

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#how-to-set-up-databricks-action-packs)

How to Set up Databricks Action Packs

1.  Open Glean Settings page
2.  Go to Platforms > Actions
3.  Click on Add button for creating a new action
4.  Click on the Databricks Actions box
5.  Populate the Configuration section
    1.  In the Default Genie Space Id text box, add the Databricks Genie space id.  
        Note: To get the Genie Space Id- when you have the Genie Space open in the Databricks UI, you can get the Genie Space Id from the URL. `https://<databricks-instance-id>.cloud.databricks.com/genie?rooms/<genie-space-id>/o=<anothernumber>`
    2.  In the Default Warehouse Id text box, add the default Databricks Warehouse Id to be used for the action.
    3.  In the Host Url text box, add the full Databricks Genie host url in the following format. Replace the databricks-instance-id with the correct ID for your Databricks instance.

*   AWS: `https://<databricks-instance-id>.cloud.databricks.com/`
*   GCP: `https://<databricks-instance-id>.gcp.databricks.com/`
*   Azure: `https://adb-<databricks-instance-id>.<number>.azuredatabricks.net/` Final Configuration Section should look like this: ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki/images/databricks-actions/image1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki&q=85&s=512152363397088f3cd9ee2a6680eab1)

6.  Populate the Authenticate section
    1.  Create OAuth app on Databricks account as per [this section](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#user-oauth-setup)
        .
    2.  Copy the Client ID and Client Secret from the OAuth app into the Authenticate section of the Action you are setting up.
    3.  Populate Client URL as `https://<AWS-or-GCP-or-Azure-Host-URL-from-step-5c>/oidc/v1/authorize`
    4.  Populate Authorization URL as `https://<AWS-or-GCP-or-Azure-Host-URL-from-step-5c>/oidc/v1/token`
    5.  Add the Scope as all-apis,offline\_access
    6.  Final Authenticate section should look like this:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki/images/databricks-actions/image2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki&q=85&s=768347f668f76da513a662e392bdfee0)
7.  Save the Action.
8.  A callback URL is generated after saving the Action. Copy that over into the Databricks OAuth app on the Databricks account console.
9.  The Action is now set up, and can be added to any app/prompt.
10.  Final Action Setup should look like this–

![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki/images/databricks-actions/image3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki&q=85&s=03736a223f8fcfedb7d1bb2b24194a97)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#user-oauth-setup)

User OAuth Setup

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#aws-databricks)

AWS Databricks

1.  Login to Databricks account
2.  Go to “Manage Account” —> “Settings” —> “App Connections”
3.  Click “Add Connection”
4.  Populate an appropriate Application Name like “Glean Databricks Genie OAuth”
5.  Add a dummy URL in the Redirect URL box.
6.  Set “Access Scopes” to “All APIs”
7.  Ensure “Generate a Client Secret” is checked
8.  Adjust the TTLs if required. Default is fine as well.
9.  Save the application.
10.  Copy the Client Id and Client Secret into the Authentication section of the Action you are setting up in [this section](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#how-to-set-up-databricks-action-packs)
    .
11.  After the Action is saved in [this section](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#how-to-set-up-databricks-action-packs)
    , a Callback URL will be generated in the Authentication section of the Action. Copy that URL.
12.  Edit the OAuth application on the Databricks account, and update it with the Callback URL from the previous step.
13.  Final OAuth app setup should look like this

![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki/images/databricks-actions/image4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1v8VopG7Y8qlR0ki&q=85&s=fe8d8eeeb411ffaf9a70f467670e27d9)

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#azure-databricks)

Azure Databricks

1.  Login to Databricks account
2.  Go to “Manage Account” —> “Settings” —> “App Connections”
3.  Click “Add Connection
4.  Populate an appropriate Application Name like “Glean Databricks Genie OAuth”
5.  Add a dummy URL in the Redirect URL box.
6.  Set “Access Scopes” to “All APIs”
7.  Ensure “Generate a Client Secret” is checked
8.  Adjust the TTLs if required. Default is fine as well.
9.  Save the application.
10.  Copy the Client Id and Client Secret into the Authentication section of the Action you are setting up in [this section](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#how-to-set-up-databricks-action-packs)
    .
11.  After the Action is saved in [this section](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/databricks-actions-setup#how-to-set-up-databricks-action-packs)
    , a Callback URL will be generated in the Authentication section of the Action. Copy that URL.
12.  Edit the OAuth application on the Databricks account, and update it with the Callback URL from the previous step.

Setup is now complete. Refer to the [Databricks end user documentation](https://docs.glean.com/agents/actions/datasource/databricks)
 for information on testing this action pack in the agent builder.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Create Redirect Actions](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/redirect-actions)
[Google Actions Setup](https://docs.glean.com/administration/assistant/actions/google-actions-setup)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Proxy_Monitor_3 - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Generic

Proxy\_Monitor\_3

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-3#issue%3A)
    
*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-3#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-3#issue%3A)

Issue:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The onprem host was not resolved to an ip address, by the proxy vm. This is required to crawl data from the on prem datasource instance.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-3#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\-There are 2 ways to resolve the host to an ip address.

1.  Set onprem.host and onprem.ip
2.  Set onprem.host and setup.proxy.nameservers.
    *   setup.proxy.nameservers should be a CSV of the nameservers which will help in resolving the onprem.host

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Proxy\_Monitor\_2](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-2)
[Proxy\_Monitor\_4](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-4)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Proxy\_Monitor\_1

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)

[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-1#issue%3A)
    
*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-1#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-1#issue%3A)

Issue:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The proxy vm is not present.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-1#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We need to enable setup.proxy.enabled config and set one of the following configs:
    *   **setup.proxy.standalone = true**
    *   **setup.sharedvpc.subnet**
    *   **setup.transit.range** If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-5#issue%3A)

Issue:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The datasource instance is not configured to use proxy.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-5#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# Action Permission Error - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Actions

Action Permission Error

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

**Issue**: When clicking “connect” in assistant response it redirect to the particular application to complete the authentication but receives redirect\_uri\_mismatch or Access blocked error. ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/actionpermission1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=631f7c78c3410acd057aa2653abe6fb3) **Error**: ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/actionpermission2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=9fc640a4a45137fd5a940cb7d066f125) **Resolution**: As the error suggests seems like the redirect url is not correctly setup. Might have not configured the correct verify\_code URI in the allowed list of redirects for the OAuth app. Below redirect url should be added in allowed URI for redirects as this endpoint exchanges the auth code for an access token.

> https://_your-glean-domain-name_\-be.glean.com/tools/oauth/verify\_code/_your-action-unique-identifier-name_

> For example: [https://acmeco-be.glean.com/tools/oauth/verify\_code/CreateGoogleDoc](https://acmeco-be.glean.com/tools/oauth/verify_code/CreateGoogleDoc)

Note: “your-action-unique-identifier-name” is case sensitive.

You can find the **your-action-unique-identifier-name** from actions setup as shown in below screenshot. ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/kv75usSCDw2F61nK/images/actionpermission3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=kv75usSCDw2F61nK&q=85&s=4a7cd2461fbc094b9df602d6fd41b73d)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Proxy\_Monitor\_5](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/generic/proxy-monitor-5)
[Google Action Errors](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/actions/google-action-erros)

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Navigation

Actions

Google Action Errors

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

While Enabling Google Actions in your Glean Admin Console, if you encounter the Error: **Error creating action pack / Service Account doesn’t have required scopes.** You need to review the Domain-wide-delegation setup permissions page and make sure the scopes are correctly defined. **Required Scopes**:

*   [https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file](https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file)
    
*   [https://www.googleapis.com/auth/gmail.compose](https://www.googleapis.com/auth/gmail.compose)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/fRXYLCZbzve_-I7o/images/googleaction1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fRXYLCZbzve_-I7o&q=85&s=a6f858f18d56ae0013245ffea25fd380)

You need to ensure you have provided Domain-wide-delegation (DWD) permissions to the service account with the client ID that pops up on the Setup instructions page while enabling Google Actions.

![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/fRXYLCZbzve_-I7o/images/googleaction2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fRXYLCZbzve_-I7o&q=85&s=8d78cabf4f1d5311b69e897e1b07f66d)

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/authentication/oauth-1#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/authentication/oauth-1#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/authentication/oauth-1#issue)

Issue
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The domain of the email used during setup must be added to your Glean account in order to authenticate. This is a security feature.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/authentication/oauth-1#resolution)

Resolution
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently adding email domains to your Glean account is not self-serve. Please work with [support@glean.com](mailto:support@glean.com)
 to add the email domain.

Atlassian

ATLASSIAN\_1

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-1#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-1#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-1#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   For Datacenter apps, the base URL entered is in an incorrect format. The Base URL should not be empty and should not end with a ”/” (slash)
*   For Cloud apps, the Atlassian domain entered is in an incorrect format.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-1#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   For Datacenter apps, please enter the base URL in the correct format.
*   For Cloud apps, please enter the Atlassian domain in the correct format. If your Atlassian instance url looks like `https://company.atlassian.net`, then your Atlassian domain is `company`.

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The Glean Crawler Application isn’t installed on your Atlassian Cloud instance

    .

    .

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The Atlassian Connect App setup will be deprecated in the future.

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please migrate to Forge App based setup, for more information refer to \[this article\] (/connectors/native/confluence/forge-upgrade).

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-7#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We are unable to establish a connection to your Confluence or Jira server.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/atlassian/atlassian-7#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Ensure that your Confluence or Jira instance is up and reachable from Glean’s VPC or over the internet.
*   This might involve setting up networking between Glean’s VPC and your onprem servers. Work with your Glean’s support to set up the connection if this is not already done or has stopped working.

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

BOX\_1

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)

[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-1#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-1#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-1#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to authenticate with Box.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-1#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Verify that your Box application has been created and configured correctly in the Box Developer Console
*   Confirm that the OAuth Client ID and OAuth Client Secret fields in Glean match the credentials from your Box application
*   Ensure that your Box application has not expired, been deleted, or disabled
*   Check that the redirect URI in your Box application settings matches what you’ve configured in Glean
*   For JWT applications: verify that the JWT private key and credentials are correctly entered and that a Box Admin has authorized the application

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-2#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-2#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-2#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We cannot access your Box user information.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-2#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In your Box Developer Console, navigate to your Box application → **Configuration** tab → **Application Scopes**
*   Ensure that **“Manage users”** is checked/enabled and save the configuration changes
*   For JWT applications: after enabling the “Manage users” scope, ensure that a Box Admin has re-authorized the application in the Box Admin Console
*   Verify that the authenticated user has Admin or Co-Admin permissions to view other users in the organization

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-3#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-3#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-3#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We cannot access information for one or more specific Box users in your configuration.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-3#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Verify that all user IDs in your Glean configuration are valid and correspond to actual users in your Box enterprise
*   In your Box Developer Console, navigate to your Box application → **Configuration** tab → **Application Scopes** and ensure **“Manage users”** is checked/enabled
*   Confirm that the authenticated user has Admin or Co-Admin permissions to access information about other users
*   Remove any user IDs for users who no longer exist or have been deleted from your Box enterprise
*   For JWT applications: ensure the application is configured with **“App Access + Enterprise Access”** application access

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# BOX_4 - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Box

BOX\_4

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-4#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-4#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-4#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Box OAuth user does not have full admin-level privileges required for Box content access.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-4#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In your Box Admin Console, navigate to **Users** → **Managed Users** and find the OAuth user account being used for the Glean integration
*   Verify that the user’s role is set to **“Admin”** (not “Co-admin”)
*   If the user is currently a Co-admin, upgrade them to full Admin status or configure Glean to use a different Box account that has full Admin privileges
*   Note: Only one user can have the Admin role, so you may need to transfer admin rights from the current Admin
*   Alternative: Consider using JWT (Server Authentication) instead of OAuth 2.0, which doesn’t have this admin role requirement

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-5#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Box application is not configured to perform actions as users.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/box/box-5#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In your Box Developer Console, navigate to your Box application → **Configuration** tab → **Advanced Features**
*   Ensure that **“Perform actions as users”** is checked/enabled and save the configuration changes
*   For JWT applications: after enabling this setting, ensure that a Box Admin has re-approved the application in the Box Admin Console

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-1#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to fetch content from your Confluence instance.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-1#resolution)

Resolution
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Confluence Cloud, make sure that the **Glean Crawler App** is installed in your Confluence instance. For Confluence Datacenter, please ensure the service account provided has the required permissions to fetch content. The service account should have VIEW access to spaces and pages within it [official documentation](https://support.atlassian.com/confluence/kb/understanding-permission-in-confluence/)
. If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

. If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-3#issue)
    
*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-3#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-3#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to fetch space permissions from your Confluence instance.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-3#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Confluence Datacenter, please ensure the service account provided has the required permissions to view space and the [Glean Activity Plugin](https://marketplace.atlassian.com/apps/1228567/glean-activity-extension-for-confluence-data-center-server?tab=installation&hosting=datacenter)
 is installed. The service account should have VIEW access to spaces that needs to be indexed (official documentation). If you are using Confluence Cloud or still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-7#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-7#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Page content redlist regex entered is invalid.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-7#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please ensure that the regex is valid. Any valid regex is accepted. For example, if you require to redlist all pages with the word “sensitive” in it, then the regex could be: `.*\b(sensitive)\b.*` If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-8#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-8#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The list provided in default access group field:

*   contains invalid/non-existent entries for groups
*   all the groups provided are empty

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-8#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please check that:
    *   all provided access groups are valid.
    *   there exists at-least one non-empty group

The membership of a product access group can be checked via admin.atlassian.com [reference](https://support.atlassian.com/user-management/docs/how-does-product-access-work/)
 If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

*   [Resolution:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-6#resolution%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-6#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to validate if redlisted creators file is uploaded correctly.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-6#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please ensure you’ve uploaded the redlisted creators with same file name as provided during setup in the sensitive configs bucket which is generally of the form: `sensitive-config-${PROJECT_ID}`
*   Please ensure that there is atleast one email added in the file. The file contains comma separated email ids which would look like: `foo@domain.com,bar@domain.com,baz@domain.com`

If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# Confluence failing to save credentials - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Confluence

Confluence failing to save credentials

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/NkMg3HtjZdwnwbZ-/images/confluencedccred1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=NkMg3HtjZdwnwbZ-&q=85&s=104ed9d9790a8013b7e0ab41672247c4) There are multiple cases in which the save credentials call fails.

1.  Check if the credentials are valid and are not expired. Sometimes, an automatic key rotation policy is enabled on the Service Accounts for security purposes.
2.  Check the response you get from the below cURL request.

Copy

    {
    curl -u username:password -X GET "https://your-confluence-url/rest/api/user?username=username_to_check"
    
    AND
    
    curl -u username:password -X GET "https://your-confluence-url/rest/api/user?username=username" -H "Content-Type: application/json"
    }
    

Ensure to add your username, and password along with your Confluence base URL in the above cURL request.

3.  Ensure the Service Account bot (for example - “scio-confluence-bot”) is active and should have access to the Confluence spaces, and has required permissions to fetch the data.
4.  Try logging/impersonating from the Service Account to your Confluence account from incognito mode to make sure the Service account can view the Confluence spaces.
5.  Check if captcha-based authentication is enabled and if the unsuccessful attempt has exceeded the limit. If that is the case then, please “Reset Failed Login Count”.

If you are still having difficulty, please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[CONFLUENCE\_8](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/confluence/confluence-8)
[DATABRICKS\_1](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/databricks/databricks-1)

Assistant

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/databricks/databricks-1#issue)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The provided OAuth Client ID of Service Principal is invalid/incorrect.
*   The provided OAuth Secret of Service Principal is invalid/incorrect.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/databricks/databricks-1#resolution)

Resolution
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please follow the setup instructions and make sure that the provided OAuth Credentials:
    *   Have been copied properly
    *   Have not expired
    *   Have not been revoked

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Issue
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The provided account url isn’t in the right format.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/databricks/databricks-4#resolution)

Resolution
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please follow the setup instructions and make sure that you copy full account url from your databricks account home page which also has the **account\_id** parameter set in it. If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Possible error](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#possible-error)
    
*   [Possible resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#possible-resolution)
    
*   [Ensure all required Dynamics 365 configuration parameters are provided during datasource setup:](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#ensure-all-required-dynamics-365-configuration-parameters-are-provided-during-datasource-setup%3A)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#possible-error)

Possible error
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Dynamics 365 configuration parameters are missing or invalid.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#possible-resolution)

Possible resolution
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To resolve this error, try the following resolution:

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-1#ensure-all-required-dynamics-365-configuration-parameters-are-provided-during-datasource-setup%3A)

Ensure all required Dynamics 365 configuration parameters are provided during datasource setup:

*   _Tenant ID (Directory ID)_: You can find the **Tenant ID** on the Azure portal by navigating to **Microsoft Entra ID** > **Overview**.
*   _Client ID (Application ID)_: You can find _Client ID_ on Azure portal by navigating to **Microsoft Entra ID** > **App registrations** > **Your Glean App** > **Overview**.
*   _Client secret_: The _Client secret_ is generated in **Microsoft Entra ID** > **App registrations** > **Your Glean App** > **Certificates & secrets** on the Azure portal.
*   _Org ID_: You can retrieve the _Org ID_ from your Dynamics 365 URL. For example, in the URL: `https://org810c0cef.crm.dynamics.com/`, the org ID is `org810c0cef`.

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)
.

[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Possible errors](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-errors)
    
*   [Possible reasons](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-reasons)
    
*   [Possible resolutions](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-resolutions)
    
*   [Generating a new client secret if the current one expired](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#generating-a-new-client-secret-if-the-current-one-expired)
    
*   [Ensuring all required permissions are added](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#ensuring-all-required-permissions-are-added)
    
*   [Granting admin consent](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#granting-admin-consent)
    
*   [Verifying application status is enabled in Azure](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#verifying-application-status-is-enabled-in-azure)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-errors)

Possible errors
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Failed to refresh access token for Dynamics 365
*   Invalid credentials provided for token authentication
*   Azure application authentication failure

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-reasons)

Possible reasons
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Client secret has expired.
*   Missing admin consent for API permissions.
*   Wrong tenant ID configuration.
*   Application disabled in Azure.
*   Network connectivity issues to `login.microsoftonline.com`.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#possible-resolutions)

Possible resolutions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To resolve this error, try one or more of the following resolutions:

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#generating-a-new-client-secret-if-the-current-one-expired)

Generating a new client secret if the current one expired

For information on generating a new client secret, see [Generate secret](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/native/microsoft/microsoft-dynamics-365-connector#5-generate-secret)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#ensuring-all-required-permissions-are-added)

Ensuring all required permissions are added

For more information on checking required permissions, see [Configure permissions](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/native/microsoft/microsoft-dynamics-365-connector#3-configure-permissions)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#granting-admin-consent)

Granting admin consent

For more information on ensuring admin consent is granted, see [Grant admin consent](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/native/microsoft/microsoft-dynamics-365-connector#4-grant-admin-consent)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-3#verifying-application-status-is-enabled-in-azure)

Verifying application status is enabled in Azure

1.  Go to **Azure** portal > **Microsoft Entra ID** > **Enterprise applications** > **All applications**.
2.  Search and select your _Enterprise application_.
3.  Open **Properties**.
4.  Confirm **Enabled for users to sign-in** is set to _Yes_.

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)
.

Dynamics 365

DYNAMICS365\_5

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)

[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Possible errors](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-errors)
    
*   [Possible reasons](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-reasons)
    
*   [Possible resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-errors)

Possible errors
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Access denied to Dynamics 365 APIs.
*   Insufficient permissions to access required Dynamics 365 endpoints.
*   Application user not properly configured in Dynamics 365.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-reasons)

Possible reasons
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Missing admin consent for Azure app permissions.
*   Application user not created in Dynamics 365 environment.
*   Insufficient security roles assigned to the application user.
*   Organization has API access restrictions.
*   Conditional access policies blocking the application.
*   Network connectivity issues with Dynamics 365 endpoints.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/dynamics365/dynamics365-5#possible-resolution)

Possible resolution
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Verify admin consent is granted for all Azure app permissions.
2.  Confirm application user exists in Dynamics 365 with appropriate roles.
3.  Test API connectivity to your Dynamics 365 organization URL.
4.  Check for any conditional access policies affecting the application.
5.  Ensure firewall or proxy allows connections to `*.dynamics.com`.

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)
.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-1#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to validate that the Glean GitHub application is installed in the customer’s GitHub organization.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-1#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please follow these instructions in order to install the Glean GitHub application in the appropriate GitHub organization.
*   If installing or updating the glean-github-app for GitHub Cloud, we’ve noticed it may take up to 10 minutes for the changes to propagate. Please wait 10 minutes and try again.

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Navigation

GitHub

GITHUB\_4

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-4#issue)
    
*   [Possible causes and resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-4#possible-causes-and-resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-4#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When setting up the Github instance, we were unable to validate that one or more of the entered repositories exist using the Repositories REST API. We allow admins to specify which repositories should be included or excluded from the content crawl and validate that they exist.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-4#possible-causes-and-resolution)

Possible causes and resolution
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For each entered repository:

*   Ensure that the full repository is included and spelled correctly. The format of the repository should be `<organization>/<repository>`, e.g. `octocat/Hello-World`
*   Ensure that the repository exists within your Github organization and is not deleted.
*   If private, ensure that the credentials provided to Glean allow us to fetch the repository.

Once updated, the changes should be reflected immediately since we are validating directly from Github’s API. If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# GITHUB_3 - Glean Help Center

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-3#issue)
    
*   [Possible causes and resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-3#possible-causes-and-resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-3#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This error occurs when Glean cannot find any organization where the GitHub App has been installed.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-3#possible-causes-and-resolution)

Possible causes and resolution
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The GitHub App has actually not been installed in any organization yet. We need the GitHub App to be installed in at least one organization so that we can validate whether other organization and repository specific endpoints are accessible.
*   The webhook URL has been misconfigured in the GitHub App. Due to this, we never receive installation events from GitHub and cannot determine when the App has been installed.
*   The webhook is received by Glean but treated as invalid due to the signature header mismatching the webhook secret Glean has stored. Please ensure that the “Webhook secret token” field in the Glean setup page matches the corresponding value stored in the GitHub App.

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-2#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-2#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-2#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’re unable to fetch GitHub resources such as members, issues, repositories, or repository content from the customer’s GitHub organization.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/github/github-2#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Ensure that the correct scopes have been granted.
*   Ensure that there is at least one of the resource that is failing. Ie the organization cannot have empty members, repositories, or issues. Issues also includes pull requests according to the GitHub API documentation.
*   If installing or updating the glean-github-app for GitHub Cloud, we’ve noticed it may take up to 10 minutes for the changes to propagate. Please wait 10 minutes and try again.

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# GITLAB_1 - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

GitLab

GITLAB\_1

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab/gitlab-1#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab/gitlab-1#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab/gitlab-1#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We were unable to fetch Gitlab users using the access token that was provided.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab/gitlab-1#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There’s a few possible reasons for this:

1.  The token does not have the read\_user scope OR the token is expired
    *   In either case, since Gitlab doesn’t allow you to view the details of a token after creation, we will have to recreate the token
    *   Head over to your Glean admin account and navigate to [https://app.glean.com/admin/setup/apps](https://app.glean.com/admin/setup/apps)
        
    *   Find your Gitlab datasource and navigate to its setup page
    *   Follow the instructions to create a new personal access token and save it
        *   Make sure to include the read\_user api scope on the token as this is the scope that allows us to fetch user information using the personal access token
2.  If the above doesn’t work, it’s possible our crawler has networking issues in reaching your Gitlab instance. Please reach out to us at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)
     to resolve this. 

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

[GITLAB\_2](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab/gitlab-2)

GitLab On-Prem

GITLAB\_3

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)

[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)

[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab-onprem/gitlab-3#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab-onprem/gitlab-3#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab-onprem/gitlab-3#issue)

Issue
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Personal Access Token (PAT) does not have the expected format. Gitlab PATs are expected to have a specific prefix and the input must be at least 20 characters long and can only contain letters (A-Z, a-z), numbers (0-9), hyphens (-), and underscores (\_). Any other characters or a shorter length is rejected.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gitlab-onprem/gitlab-3#resolution)

Resolution
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Ensure the token you are entering is a valid PAT.

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gmail/gmail-2#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gmail/gmail-2#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gmail/gmail-2#issue)

Issue
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Could not connect to Gmail service.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gmail/gmail-2#resolution)

Resolution
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Gmail uses the Directory Admin configured for the associated Google Drive instance. Ensure a Directory Admin e-mail is set in the associated Google Drive instance and that this is a valid email account on the Gmail service.
*   Ensure the Gmail Service is active.
*   Ensure that correct scopes have been granted.

For additional assistance, please contact Glean Support at [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-1#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-1#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-1#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to fetch an access token for a required API scope. The error message displayed in the console should display the specific scope we’re missing.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-1#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Head to [https://admin.google.com/u/1/ac/owl/domainwidedelegation](https://admin.google.com/u/1/ac/owl/domainwidedelegation)
     and ensure the client ID displayed in the error message has been granted the specified API scope
*   Also verify that the app with the same client ID is ‘Trusted’ here: [https://admin.google.com/ac/owl/list?tab=configuredApps](https://admin.google.com/ac/owl/list?tab=configuredApps)
    .
*   For more information on the specified API scope: [https://developers.google.com/drive/api/guides/api-specific-auth](https://developers.google.com/drive/api/guides/api-specific-auth)
    

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-3#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-3#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-3#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The directory admin account you entered is missing privileges to list shared drives.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-3#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Verify that the directory admin email you entered is valid and is an admin who has access to shared drives.
*   If you have created a custom admin role, verify that the role you created has the following “Admin Console Privilege”: **Services > Drive and Docs > Settings**

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-5#issue)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-5#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

POC group is not set up correctly.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-5#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check that the POC group is:

*   not empty
*   not nested i.e. has no sub-groups
*   not larger than maximum number of allowed members (default: 100)

If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

# GDRIVE-2 - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

Navigation

Google Drive

GDRIVE-2

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Issue](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-2#issue)
    
*   [Resolution](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-2#resolution)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-2#issue)

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are unable to make an API request for a required API scope. The error message displayed in the console should display the specific scope we’re unable to validate.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-2#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Verify that the directory admin user is setup correctly**

*   In your Google Admin console (at [admin.google.com](http://admin.google.com/)
    ),
*   Go to [Menu > Directory > Users](https://admin.google.com/ac/users)
    .
*   Search for the directory admin email and navigate to the user’s page
*   Verify that the user has the right privileges
    *   Under Admin roles and privileges > Privileges, verify that the user has all the right privileges that are [here](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1I67s1U6iViZdwlOm1JI-mM5jS4hhAR_1MBqkJfb11DY/edit#bookmark=id.b74k05pbc8mi)
        
*   Verify that the user has logged in at least once in to Google Workspace and accepted the Terms of Service
*   Verify that the user has access to the GDrive app
    
    *   Under Apps, verify that **Drive and Docs** is ON
    
    ![](https://support.glean.com/hc/article_attachments/26479059048603)
    

**Verify that the Drive SDK is available to the user**

*   On the admin portal ([admin.google.com](http://admin.google.com/)
    ), from the left sidebar click Apps → Google Workspace → Drive and Docs
*   Then click Features and Applications, and under Users search for the directory admin email
*   Verify that under Drive SDK, the setting Allow users to access Google Drive with the Drive SDK API is ON
    
    ![](https://support.glean.com/hc/article_attachments/26479059048603)
    

For more information on the specified API scope: [https://developers.google.com/drive/api/guides/api-specific-auth](https://developers.google.com/drive/api/guides/api-specific-auth)
 If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[GDRIVE-1](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-1)
[GDRIVE-3](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-3)

Assistant

Issue
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-6#resolution)

Resolution
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

, and verify that all of the domains you entered are present in this list without misspellings. If you are still having difficulty please reach out to us: [https://support.glean.com](https://support.glean.com/)

Issue:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/error-codes/gdrive/gdrive-8#resolution%3A)

Resolution:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Either supply an existing user from the Google Workspace that has the necessary permissions OR create a new user under that google workspace with the necessary permissions and supply that email instead.
