[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/extension-sidebar#glean-browser-extension-sidebar)

Glean browser extension sidebar
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Glean browser extension sidebar enhances your research and discovery capabilities directly within your web browser on both indexed and unindexed web pages. It consolidates essential functionalities into an interface accessible via keyboard shortcuts or the Glean icon. The sidebar features two distinct tabs:

*   **Chat tab:** Provides an AI assistant that uses contextual and company knowledge to enhance research.
*   **Search tab:** Enables searches for relevant content, documents, and experts.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/extension-sidebar#using-the-sidebar-screenshot)

Using the sidebar screenshot
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Capture and use content that can’t be copied or highlighted on the web page.

*   Screenshot images, non-selectable text, or specific sections from the current page in just a few clicks.
*   Add screenshots to Collections, or share in chat for context and seamless collaboration with your team.
*   Focus on part of a page and bring more content into Glean’s chat and tools.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/extension-sidebar#accessing-the-sidebar)

Accessing the sidebar
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are three ways to access the Glean browser extension sidebar:

*   Use the keyboard shortcut: Command + J (Mac) or Alt + J (Windows).
*   Click the blue Glean icon on the sticky tab on the right side of the screen.
*   Navigate to the Glean extension icon (puzzle piece) in the navigation bar.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/extension-sidebar#knowledge-tools)

Knowledge tools
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The content tab provides knowledge tools that enhance your ability to organize and access information:

*   **Collections:** Add or view collections this document is relevant to, helping you organize related content for easy discovery later.
*   **Go Links:** Create or view Go Links to the current page you are on, enabling quick access through memorable shortcuts.

# Info Access - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Glean Assistant

Info Access

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Glean Search](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#glean-search)
    
*   [Glean Chat](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#glean-chat)
    
*   [Influencing Results](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#influencing-results)
    

Glean gathers information from multiple sources to create unique responses based on several inputs, such as your access permissions, search and chat settings, prompt, and any additional information you provide in the chat box. Just as every person is unique, so are their search results! Glean offers two distinct methods for searching content: Glean Chat and Glean Search. Depending on your needs, you might prefer one over the other.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#glean-search)

Glean Search

Glean Search functions like a traditional search engine. You enter a query and receive results that you can explore independently. This method is useful when you want to browse through various documents and information sources.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#glean-chat)

Glean Chat

Glean Chat acts as a conversational tool where you can ask questions and receive answers. There are two types of chat modes in Glean: Company Knowledge and World Knowledge:

*   **Company Knowledge** Uses the underlying large language model alongside your accessible company data to provide responses. When using Company Knowledge, Glean’s sources include the LLM’s inherent knowledge and the files within your company that you have access to.
*   **World Knowledge** Uses the underlying large language model to provide responses based on general world knowledge. In World Mode, you can enhance the LLM’s understanding by selecting the Web Search option when typing your query, allowing Glean to search the internet for answers and incorporate the results into its responses. When using World Knowledge, Glean’s sources include the LLM’s inherent knowledge and the internet.

You can control what information Glean accesses by selecting **Company Knowledge**, **World Knowledge**, or the **Web Search** option with world knowledge in the chat box.

Web search is only available if your administrator has enabled it.

Glean personalizes search results based on your activity and the permissions set in your company’s data sources. This means that the results you see are tailored to the documents and information you have access to and have interacted with. For example, if you frequently access certain documents or collaborate with specific colleagues, those documents and related content are more likely to appear in your search results. Your coworker might have different access permissions or have interacted with different documents, leading to different responses. To better understand how Glean integrates information based on your selections, refer to the following diagram: ![](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/different-chat-modes.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=b173d2272163c2394df71494685e2758)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/how-glean-accesses-info#influencing-results)

Influencing Results

You can create collections and verify documents to influence the likelihood they will be used in results. Glean respects the permissions set in your company’s data sources. If you have permission to view a document in Google Drive or a thread in a public Slack channel, it will appear in your search results. If your coworker has different permissions, they might see different results. Additionally, if any permissions change, Glean’s results will reflect those changes quickly. Glean’s responses can vary even for the same query, depending on the chat settings and the context of previous interactions. By understanding these features, you can effectively utilize Glean Search and Glean Chat to find the information you need efficiently.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#what-is-an-advanced-prompt-and-when-should-i-create-one%3F)

What is an Advanced Prompt and when should I create one?
================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Simple Prompts will only perform one round of retrieval per request, which is either searching for documents/people or reading the full contents of documents from the Glean index. Advanced Prompts enable you to complete more complex tasks that require multiple retrieval steps, including being able to chain together dependent retrieval steps. For example, you can search for Jiras related to an issue and then instruct the Assistant to read the full contents of those Jiras. Advanced Prompts also give you more explicit control over which searches to issue, which can make task execution more deterministic. For more information, see our blog post about [Next-generation Prompting](https://www.glean.com/blog/glean-prompting-product)
 and [demos of Advanced Prompts](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AIvtJV3cLz4)
.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#getting-started)

Getting started
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From [Glean Chat](https://app.glean.com/chat)
, click on the **Create Prompt** button in the top right to load the Prompt Builder. Then click on the **Advanced** toggle at the top of the Prompt Builder. ![Advanced Prompt Interface](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=b32600b1b15c696e2bc973110148bd3c)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#anatomy-of-an-advanced-prompt)

Anatomy of an advanced prompt
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An Advanced Prompt has 3 main components, which we’ll discuss below.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#goal)

Goal

This specifies the high level outcome you want to achieve in natural language. Examples:

*   Create a report of tickets that request a specific feature
*   Extract information from call transcripts with a customer

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#steps)

Steps

An Advanced Prompt can have 2 or more steps. Every step executes its own **action** which will load information into the **memory** that can be accessed by any subsequent step. Here are some actions you can use:

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#glean-search)

Glean search

This will search for documents in the Glean index and will load snippets from the search results into the memory. You can specify the request in natural language (the pencil icon) and the system will make its best effort to convert this into one or more Glean searches. ![Glean Search](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=6144f892e038da96614dc9e080ec7760) Alternatively, you can make the Glean search step faster and more deterministic by clicking on the parameters icon to explicitly specify the search query templates. These can be any search query that you can enter into Glean and can include facets like “app:” and “updated:“ ![Glean Search Parameters](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=24b0db8a63e598f089c6817b12b88d18)

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#employee-search)

Employee search

This will search for people in your organization by either information about their role or their expertise.

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#read-documents)

Read documents

This reads the full contents of one or more documents and loads them into the memory. If you already know which documents you want to read, it is best to use the input templates (via the parameters icon) where you can either enter their URLs or type @ to tag a recently accessed document. ![Read Documents](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=17a85dacfe2cd9123e46938605135ef0) Another use case is to read the documents found by Glean Search in a previous step. In this case, you would enter natural language instructions (via the pencil icon) that specify the criteria for which documents to read. Example: ![Read Documents Example](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=69168c7fbe30882f4b33eccb34316fff)

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#generate-response)

Generate response

These are natural language instructions for generating a response from all the information that’s currently in the memory. This is usually the last step in an Advanced Prompt and is the only action that outputs natural language text to the user. Example: ![Generate Response](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=6ffef2cd6251698110b54bd3587b506d)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/assistant/prompt-library/guide-to-advanced-prompts#input-fields)

Input Fields

In any input box, including Goal, you can create a field by enclosing it in double brackets \[\[ and \]\]. Examples:

*   Find Gong calls with \[\[customer\]\] from the past month
*   Find Slack messages that mention \[\[project name\]\] from the past week

The system will automatically outline the input field in blue and will add it to the **Fields** section at the top of the prompt. You can then test the prompt with different values for the input fields.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/chat/guide-to-advanced-prompts)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Installing the browser extension](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/installing-the-browser-extension)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

On this page

*   [I want to go back to my old blank browser new tab:](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#i-want-to-go-back-to-my-old-blank-browser-new-tab%3A)
    
*   [I want to go back to my previous custom new tab (e.g. Momentum, Scratchpad, Earth View):](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#i-want-to-go-back-to-my-previous-custom-new-tab-e-g-momentum%2C-scratchpad%2C-earth-view-%3A)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#what-is-glean%3F)

What is Glean?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Glean is the AI-powered workplace assistant that searches all of your apps across your entire company, understanding context, language behavior, and relationships with others, to find personalized answers to all your workplace questions. You can read more about what we do and how to use us [here](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#how-did-glean-become-my-new-tab-page%3F)

How did Glean become my new tab page?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Glean extension was installed into your browser by your company which has vetted the product’s effectiveness, security, and ability to save you time.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#how-can-i-get-my-old-new-tab-page-back%3F)

How can I get my old new tab page back?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Although the Glean new tab page is an essential part of finding what you need from all your tools and quickly accessing relevant content, we understand sometimes you just want your old new tab back.

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#i-want-to-go-back-to-my-old-blank-browser-new-tab%3A)

I want to go back to my old blank browser new tab:

After you log in to Glean, on the home or new tab page, click the **Home page** **settings icon** in the top right corner to open the settings panel. From there, you can turn off Glean as your new tab entirely by flipping the toggle.

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#i-want-to-go-back-to-my-previous-custom-new-tab-e-g-momentum%2C-scratchpad%2C-earth-view-%3A)

I want to go back to my previous custom new tab (e.g. Momentum, Scratchpad, Earth View):

If you had a previous extension that replaced your new tab and prefer that over Glean, you’ll have to uninstall the extension that gave you that previous new tab experience (Momentum, Scratchpad, Earth View, etc). Then, reinstall that same extension and your previous new tab should be restored.

#### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-extension-via-company-push#how-can-i-continue-to-use-glean%3F)

How can I continue to use Glean?

After you’ve reset your new tab, don’t forget that there are other entry points for Glean!

*   Typing \*\*`gl`\*\*in the address bar followed by your search
*   CMD + J for the sidebar
*   [app.glean.com](https://app.glean.com/)
    
*   [Desktop app](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app)
    

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/faq/glean-extension-via-company-push)
.

YesNo

# Searching from the address bar - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Advanced

Searching from the address bar

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Chrome](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/searching-from-address-bar#chrome)
    
*   [Firefox](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/searching-from-address-bar#firefox)
    

You will need the [Glean Extension](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/installing-the-browser-extension)
 installed to use this feature.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/searching-from-address-bar#chrome)

Chrome
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Chrome, just type **`gl`** **`space`** or **`gl`** **`tab`** into the address bar, followed by your query in Glean. ![Chrome Glean Search](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=c57b695dd0cc2809a7959ef1620a037a) If you also start typing “app.glean…”, you can also tab to search directly in Glean from there.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/searching-from-address-bar#firefox)

Firefox
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to [app.glean.com](http://app.glean.com/)
 and click into the address bar. Right click, and you’ll see an option to **Add “Glean”** at the bottom of the menu. ![Firefox Add Glean Search](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=653f7109d916cf0442049e5e15ade1b3) You can also click into the address bar, and click on the Glean icon in the bottom row of the menu (with the green plus button). ![Firefox Glean Icon](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=36f04ef91d6bf2562fa150fa697a3edf) Then, navigate to the search section, under your Firefox Preferences (or just type **about:preferences#search** into the address bar). Double click on “Glean” in the list, and you’ll be able to add your own keyword there. ![Firefox Search Preferences](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=628ac7c80ad583a00d6af23d9b34827f) We recommend setting this up at @gl (short, easy to type). ![Firefox Glean Keyword](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=f4558ba8d98f67033cf3c3893d0485c3) You’ll then be able to search directly with Glean from the address bar! ![Firefox Glean Search Result](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/advanced/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=9e7ba642073e456d6335173f76f8c1db)

After opening a new window/Firefox tab, pressing the tab button will not focus on the Glean search box. Unfortunately, this is a known problem on the Firefox end. Please use `F6 + Tab` to focus on the Glean search box.

Looking for the original versions of this page? You can find the archived versions [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/faq/pressing-tab-is-not-focusing-on-glean-search-box-in-firefox)
 and [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/faq/how-do-i-search-glean-directly-from-the-address-bar)
.

# Customizing Your Glean Home Page - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Advanced

Customizing Your Glean Home Page

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Navigating to the Preferences Menu](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#navigating-to-the-preferences-menu)
    
*   [Appearance](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#appearance)
    
*   [Theme](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#theme)
    
*   [Wallpaper](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#wallpaper)
    
*   [Layout](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#layout)
    
*   [General](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#general)
    
*   [Default composer selection](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#default-composer-selection)
    
*   [Tips](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#tips)
    

Your Glean home page is fully customizable to match your workflow, aesthetic preferences, and productivity needs. Here’s a guide to the settings available under **Home Page Preferences**, and what each one does.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#navigating-to-the-preferences-menu)

Navigating to the Preferences Menu
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Go to the Glean Home Page:** Use [app.glean.com](http://app.glean.com/)
    
2.  **Open the Settings Panel:** Click the user menu settings (slider filter icon) on the top right side of the homepage

You will see a drawer open on the right hand side containing all the customization options.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#appearance)

**Appearance**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose how your home page looks and feels.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#theme)

Theme

*   **Light**: A bright, classic look.
*   **Dark**: A sleek, low-light theme that’s easy on the eyes.
*   **System**: Automatically matches your operating system’s light or dark mode setting.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#wallpaper)

Wallpaper

Choose from a variety of static and scenic wallpapers to personalize your background.

*   Tap any image to apply it.
*   To remove wallpaper, select the blank option in the top-left.
*   **Surprise me**: Check this box to cycle through a new wallpaper every day.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#layout)

**Layout**
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize how content is displayed on your home page.

*   **Simple**: A minimal and focused layout—great if you prefer a clean workspace.
*   **Informational** (default): Displays helpful widgets like your calendar, mentions, trending content, and more.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#general)

**General**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Control basic behavior of the Glean home page.

*   **Use Glean as new tab page**: When toggled on, Glean will appear every time you open a new tab in your browser.
*   **Show bookmarks bar**: Toggle this to show or hide the bookmarks bar for quick access to saved links.
*   **Show shortcuts**: Toggle this to show or hide shortcuts to commonly visited pages or apps.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#default-composer-selection)

**Default composer selection**
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose the default mode for the composer (the box where you type search queries or chat prompts) each time you load the Home Page. This gives you faster access to your preferred workflow, whether you’re a search power user or rely on Glean Assistant for chat.

*   **Search (default)**: Composer defaults to a search mode—ideal if you primarily use Glean for quick lookups.
*   **Chat** : Composer opens ready for a conversation with Glean’s assistant.
*   **Sticky:** Glean will remember your last used mode—Search or Chat—and default to that next time.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/customizing-home-page#tips)

Tips
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Changes take effect immediately—no need to save.
*   You can return to this settings panel anytime to make updates.
*   If you’re not sure what to pick, try “Surprise me” for wallpapers and “Informational” layout for maximum utility.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Keyboard Shortcuts](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/advanced/keyboard-shortcuts)

# Glean companion - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Glean companion

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)

On this page

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-companion#introduction)

Introduction
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Glean companion provides seamless access to your company’s knowledge and insights directly within your browser. This floating widget contextualizes any text you highlight, allowing you to quickly understand terms, find related information, identify experts, improve your writing, summarize content, and translate text without leaving your current application or document. ![glean-companion-0](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/apps/glean-companion-0.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=b077cfd5a85fe3c48ecee8391398d406)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-companion#using-glean-companion)

Using Glean companion
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To activate the companion, simply highlight any text in your browser. A Glean icon will appear next to the highlighted text. Clicking this icon opens companion, offering six key functionalities:

*   **Explain**: Highlight any unfamiliar term or technical phrase to understand its meaning within your company’s context.
*   **Find related documents**: Highlight a short phrase to discover relevant documents indexed in Glean that discuss similar concepts.
*   **Find experts**: Highlight a key concept to identify subject matter experts on that topic within your organization.
*   **Improve writing**: Highlight a sentence or paragraph to have Glean refine and rewrite the content for grammar and clarity.
*   **Summarize this**: Highlight a paragraph or an entire page to generate a concise summary.
*   **Translate**: Translate any highlighted text into 13 different languages.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-companion#getting-started)

Getting Started
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Glean companion is accessible by downloading the [Glean browser extension](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/installing-the-browser-extension)
. For troubleshooting, please contact your Glean representative.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/glean-companion#managing-glean-companion)

Managing Glean companion
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Disabling companion on a specific webpage**: To disable companion on a particular website, highlight any text to activate it, click the Power icon, and select ‘Hide for this site’.
*   **Disabling companion**: To disable companion across all webpages, navigate to the Glean sidebar settings (command+J on macOS or alt+J on Windows) and toggle off the companion option within the companion settings.
*   **Data privacy**: Glean companion does not automatically read the content of webpages. It only accesses content when you explicitly highlight text and invoke the feature. Glean does not store any personal information through companion and strictly adheres to its 30-day data retention policy.
*   **Default availability**: Glean companion will be automatically enabled on these web pages. Additional permissions can be granted to have the Glean Companion be available on all web pages.

Copy

    https://app.box.com/*
    https://*.asana.com/*
    https://*.atlassian.net/*
    https://*.docebosaas.com/*
    https://docs.google.com/*
    https://*.docusign.com/*

# Configuring dark mode - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Advanced

Configuring dark mode

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

Glean supports dark mode across its desktop and mobile applications to allow users to tailor their experience. This guide will help you understand what options Glean provides, as well as how to configure them. By default, Glean will mirror your system’s settings. When your computer or phone is set to dark mode, Glean will also be in dark mode. You can also set Glean to remain in dark mode or light mode by navigating to [your settings](https://app.glean.com/settings)
 and selecting the appropriate option. Glean applies these preferences across its desktop, [Android](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.glean.app)
 and [iOS](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/glean-work/id1582892407)
 apps. You can change these settings at any time.

# Why does the Chrome extension ask for those permissions? - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Glean Apps

Why does the Chrome extension ask for those permissions?

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Read and change all your data on websites you visit](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-all-your-data-on-websites-you-visit)
    
*   [Replace the page you see when opening a new tab](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#replace-the-page-you-see-when-opening-a-new-tab)
    
*   [Read and change your browsing history](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-your-browsing-history)
    
*   [Read and change your bookmarks](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-your-bookmarks)
    

You might’ve noticed our Chrome Extension asks for several permissions you might be unfamiliar with, so let’s break down the details together.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-all-your-data-on-websites-you-visit)

Read and change all your data on websites you visit

Glean has a variety of features that enhance the user experience and shown in the native tool. Some examples are:

*   Native search replacement where Glean powers search directly in tools like Atlassian and Drive
*   Our Glean sticky tab appears on workplace apps where you can verify a document.
*   To use [Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work)
    , it asks for an additional permission to read and change your data on “go,” which enables redirection to shortened links

In order to provide these features, it requires this broad permission – but the access is limited to only workplace applications that work with Glean.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#replace-the-page-you-see-when-opening-a-new-tab)

Replace the page you see when opening a new tab

We replace your new tab page with our search experience so you can bring up anything from any tool you use in an instant. You can still search Google from the browser’s URL bar or disable Glean acting as the new tab at any time from the settings.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-your-browsing-history)

Read and change your browsing history

We only use the “read” part of this permission so we can autocomplete search results for you and and improve search result ranking for individual users. The system only uses history from the workplace apps you’ve connected to Glean and other well known productivity apps that we don’t currently index (e.g. Notion, Airtable, etc), and ignore all other history. This data will never be shared with any 3rd party.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/why-does-the-chrome-extension-ask-for-those-permissions#read-and-change-your-bookmarks)

Read and change your bookmarks

We show a dismissible bookmarks bar on our new tab page, since replacing Chrome’s default new tab page also disables the Google bookmarks feature which only shows the bookmarks bar on a new tab.

YesNo

On this page

*   [About the desktop app](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#about-the-desktop-app)
    
*   [Setting up the app](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#setting-up-the-app)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#about-the-desktop-app)

About the desktop app

Glean’s desktop app brings the power of Glean to your Mac, whenever you need it. Invoke Glean from any application using _Cmd-Shift-J_, and type your query to run a search or start a chat conversation with Glean Assistant. ![get-the-desktop-app-0](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app-0.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=b4b46932613557ab8bd04dd203dfc535)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#setting-up-the-app)

Setting up the app

You can download the desktop app from the [Mac App Store](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/glean-desktop/id6448766375)
 or [directly from Glean](https://storage.googleapis.com/glean-downloads/glean-desktop-app/Glean.pkg)
. After installing the app, you will have to sign in to Glean. In the app’s settings, you can make the following adjustments to your experience:

*   **Quick search shortcut** controls the keyboard shortcut that opens up the quick search bar anywhere on your Mac. it is _Cmd-Shift-J_ by default, but can be changed to any desired key combination.
*   **Hide menu bar icon** hides the Glean menu bar icon when enabled.
*   **Hide from dock** hides the Glean icon from appearing in the Dock. If the app is pinned to the Dock, its icon will not be hidden, even if this setting is enabled.
*   **Open quick search results in browser** will cause search and chat queries from the quick search bar to open in your default browser, rather than the Glean app window, similar to Apple’s default Spotlight behavior.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#important-notes%3A)

Important notes:

*   Glean will not search local files, such as content on your desktop.
*   The app is only available for macOS 10.15 (“Catalina”) or later. We do not currently have a Windows app.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/apps/get-the-desktop-app#controlling-automatic-updates)

Controlling automatic updates

We provide system preferences to control automatic updates. You can disable automatic updates on a per-user basis. This may be helpful for testing new versions of the app before releasing them, or for gradually rolling out app updates. To maintain app reliability and security, we recommend updating Glean whenever a new app version is released. To prevent Glean from automatically checking for updates, run the following terminal command as each user who will be running the Glean desktop app:

Copy

    defaults write /Users/$USER/Library/Preferences/com.glean.desktop GleanNoAutoUpdates -bool YES
    

Use the following command to re-enable automatic updates:

Copy

    defaults write /Users/$USER/Library/Preferences/com.glean.desktop GleanNoAutoUpdates -bool NO
    

By default, automatic updates will be enabled.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#what-are-answers%3F)

What are Answers?
=======================================================================================================================================

Answers are bite-sized chunks of information you create in Glean to answer common questions your teammates - and future teammates - might have. Let’s take a look at how they work.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#create-an-answer)

Create an answer
===================================================================================================================================

Anyone can create Answers in Glean - either in the web product or via the Glean Slackbot.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#create-an-answer-in-the-web-product)

Create an answer in the web product
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the **Answers page** in the top navigation and then on the **New answer** button on that page. ![Answers Page](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=1a18f01b85b5e41e5979954cc7e32358) Answers have an associated question and can include free-form text, links, and formatting via markdown. You can also add:

*   Audience - Target your answer to appear to members of a department
*   Collections - Put your answer in a collection to organize it with other documents and answers of a certain topic, e.g. “Benefits” or “Onboarding”
*   Editors - Add other people who can also edit your answer

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#create-an-answer-via-the-slackbot)

Create an answer via the Slackbot
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Busy answering questions asked directly on Slack? We’ve made it easy for you to turn those messages on Slack directly into an Answer in Glean, so you can just answer a question once and point people to Glean in the future. On any message, simply click on the `...` button and click on the **“Create an answer in Glean”** message action. ![Slack Message Action](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=7e39e07c12bc7fc7696c17a92a642469) You may not see the option available in the menu at first, so click on **“More message shortcuts”** and search for **answer**. In the future, you’ll see this option directly in the menu. In the “Create an answer” modal that appears, the answer section will be prefilled with the message from which you created the Answer. Edit that to your liking and add a question and optional tags - then you’re good to go! ![Create Answer Modal](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=04408cdba067849463b75ad18df49d78)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#see-answers-in-search-results)

See Answers in search results
=============================================================================================================================================================

When others search for queries that match your question, they’ll see your answer in their results. If we’re highly confident in an answer based on your query, we’ll show that answer at the top of the results page: ![Top Result Answer](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=dd87c6b036bb92ce88863d1fb947d8a2) Otherwise, you’ll see Answers blended in with other results using our ranking magic! ![Blended Results](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=9fff75a041dce8d9695bcc58a5524078) You’ll also see answers in results if you use the `/glean` command on Slack.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/what-are-answers-and-how-do-they-work#how-do-i-get-started%3F)

How do I get started?
===============================================================================================================================================

Check out: [How to write effective answers](http://help.askscio.com/en/articles/4296990-how-to-write-effective-answers)

# How To Write Effective Answers - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Answers

How To Write Effective Answers

[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [1\. Think of common questions you or your team get asked](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#1-think-of-common-questions-you-or-your-team-get-asked)
    
*   [2\. Phrase your question completely](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#2-phrase-your-question-completely)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#1-think-of-common-questions-you-or-your-team-get-asked)

1\. Think of common questions you or your team get asked
==========================================================================================================================================================================================================

These might be a category of questions (i.e. “Where is XYZ”), questions related to a workflow, or questions that come up at certain times of the year. **Some examples to get you started 👇**

*   Where can I find…?
*   What existing work has been done on…?
*   What’s our process for…?
*   What’s the policy for…?
*   How do I configure…?
*   How do I set up…?
*   How do I troubleshoot…?

**Pro tip ✨** If your team has a public Slack channel that others use to collaborate with/ask questions of your team, or a private Slack channel for questions among yourselves, look through that for ideas. Adding answers for those kinds of questions will save time for you and your teammates in the future!

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#2-phrase-your-question-completely)

2\. Phrase your question completely
================================================================================================================================================================

In the **New Answer** modal, write your question in a complete sentence. When others search for that question or keywords/queries that match the question, they’ll see your answer at the top of their results. Your question will also be used as a **title** for your answer.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#3-write-your-answer)

3\. Write your answer
====================================================================================================================================

You can add a link, text, or both to your answer. The way your answers looks in the text editor is exactly like how others will see your answer at the top of their search results. ![Answer Creation Interface](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=333fbf9b65035c25e48e7a7a2df05555) Then just save and you’re done! You can always edit your answer from the search results, or click **Answers** in the top navigation bar to view and edit your answers.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers#other-ways-to-create-answers)

Other ways to create answers
====================================================================================================================================================

**Create answer from result** Use this if you’ve already searched for something, and see a result you want to appear at the top for everyone when they search for the same thing. Hover over the result, click the “more” menu with the three dots, and click **Create Answer**. ![Create Answer Option](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=30b9c15659266e81f318a5906704ed03)

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/answers/how-to-write-effective-answers)
.

# Setting up Team Pages - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Teams

Setting up Team Pages

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Setup process:](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/setting-up-team-pages#setup-process%3A)
    

It can be hard to coordinate efforts between groups of people at your company, and Glean’s teams pages are here to help. These pages provide a single hub for people at your company to learn about who’s working together, and what they’re working on. This help article will guide you through the process of setting up teams; for more information on how to use team pages, see [this article](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages)
. _Note:_ _Only admins and users with team moderator permissions can set up teams._ Users can access teams pages through search, by clicking on teams in user profiles, and by visiting the team directory. All members of a team will be able to edit that page, including its name, description, profile photo, banner photo, contact information and which members are listed as leads on the team page. Users can be in multiple teams at once. That way, one person can be in a team for their department, the DevOps pod they’re working in and an employee resource group they’re a part of. Glean recommends – at a minimum – setting up teams pages for every department. After that, we see additional value from creating teams that match your company’s internal structure Once you have teams set up in your organization, Glean recommends enlisting individual team leads to update their teams’ contents, including photos, descriptions, and preferred contact methods. (Those leads are welcome to delegate those tasks as necessary, but they have the best context for what to create.) From there, users should begin seeing the teams pages as they use Glean normally.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/setting-up-team-pages#setup-process%3A)

Setup process:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a new team, go to the team dashboard in Glean’s Directory tab. Click on the “new team” button in the upper right-hand corner, and then follow the prompts to go about creating teams from there. We currently support creating teams from two sources:

*   **Slack**: All public slack channels connected to the Glean instance can be used to create teams where all channel members will be part of the team.
    *   Note: Slackentgrid is not supported as a team source.
*   **People data in Glean**: You can also create teams from eligible fields (e.g. department, role, location, and/or team) in your company’s people data. This data is typically populated from your single sign-on system, such as Google Workspace, Okta or Azure Active Directory.You can use multiple people data fields to create teams, so your company can have pages based on departments, locations and other facets.

While not recommended, Glean also supports manually creating teams through our Push API. For more information on that, contact your Account Manager or Delivery Excellence Manager. Once a team has been created in the teams dashboard, it may take up to an hour to appear in search results for all users. In the meantime, admins can view all teams (including those queued for creation) on the teams dashboard. The teams dashboard supports the following functions:

*   Searching for a team by name
*   Filtering for a team based on department or business unit
*   Ordering teams based on name, data source (e.g Slack, people data in Glean), created from (for Slack this is the channel name, for people fields this is the field name), and last updated (the last time a team page has been edited)Note that all teams being created or deleted will show up first in the dashboard while Glean is processing them.
*   Bulk deletion of teams

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

# Celebrations Widget - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Celebrations Widget

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#what-is-the-celebrations-widget%3F)

What is the celebrations widget?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The celebrations widget helps you and your teammates celebrate each other by recognizing new hires and work anniversaries. The celebration widget appears in the right-hand column of the Glean home page and displays a carousel of teammates who have reached a new work anniversary or recently joined the team. ![Celebrations Widget](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/what-is-the-celebrations-widget-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=fb6ebe619397947e69ea45bc4ef2283c)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#how-can-i-congratulate-my-teammate%3F)

How can I congratulate my teammate?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can click on the “say welcome/congrats” button to send a message to the celebrated teammate through your organization’s chat application such as Slack or Teams. If the teammate does not have a Slack or Teams profile, clicking on the button will launch your organization’s email application instead.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#who-shows-up-on-my-widget%3F)

Who shows up on my widget?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Glean will display up to 10 celebrations in the widget at any time. The selection is personalized, so you will see celebrations for teammates with whom you have a relationship. Cards will be visible for the entire week of the celebration.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#what-determines-the-order-of-the-celebrations-shown-on-the-widget%3F)

What determines the order of the celebrations shown on the widget?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are being celebrated, your card will always appear first. Next, the widget will show teammates who have anniversaries or new start dates today, followed by teammates who have upcoming anniversaries, and then teammates whose anniversaries have past.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#i-don%E2%80%99t-want-others-to-know-about-my-celebration-how-do-i-opt-out%3F)

I don’t want others to know about my celebration. How do I opt out?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Select “Your settings” from the avatar dropdown menu. ![Your Settings](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/what-is-the-celebrations-widget-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=7a29236c59c2c63655b46435814093a8)
2.  Under “Privacy,” toggle off the option to feature your celebrations on the home page. ![Privacy Settings](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/what-is-the-celebrations-widget-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=9cb1a8bb3ffd38a6d35a9fb5560206b9)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/celebrations-widget#where-does-the-celebration-data-come-from%3F)

Where does the celebration data come from?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The celebrations widget uses start date data from your company’s people data source (HR or IT system) to determine when to showcase particular teammates. If that source data is incorrect, you will see celebrations appear on incorrect days.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/faq/what-is-the-celebrations-widget)
.

# How Go Links Work - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Go Links

How Go Links Work

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)

On this page

*   [What are Go Links?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#what-are-go-links%3F)
    
*   [How to create a Go Link](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#how-to-create-a-go-link)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#what-are-go-links%3F)

What are Go Links?
======================================================================================================================

Go Links are a way to create short memorable links for important URLs at your company in the form of **go/link**. Go Links act like a mental bookmark: once you see it or hear it, you immediately know how to access it, both now and in the future. For example, you could create **go/401k** for your company’s 401k portal, **go/it-help** for your IT help desk, or **go/sprint-planning** for your Jira project. Glean also supports [Variable Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links)
 and [appending Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/uncategorized/appending-go-links.mdx)
 that allows you to access hundreds of specific destinations using a single Go Link. _**Important:**_ _Go Links are supported via the [Glean browser extension](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/glean/cfpdompphcacgpjfbonkdokgjhgabpij)
 or via DNS redirection._ _If you have the extension installed, you’ll see a prompt to grant permissions at the top of [Tools > Go Links](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
. If you’d like to set up DNS-based Go Links redirection, Please contact our Sales or Customer Success team._

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#how-to-create-a-go-link)

How to create a Go Link
==============================================================================================================================

![Go Links Creation Process](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=f831337f1b614a200645e6175bc822f6)

1.  Paste the URL you’d like this Go Link to redirect to under Destination URL.
2.  Name the Go Link (what appears after **go/\_\_\_\_**).
3.  Add an optional description of what the link refers to so it’s easier to maintain over time.

The name of a Go Link must be unique and is limited to **letters, numbers, dashes, underscores, colons, periods, ampersands, and forward slashes.** When you navigate to a Go Link, we’ll ignore dashes and underscores. This helps people get to the right destination even if they don’t remember the exact Go Link name. For example, **go/q4-goals**, **go/q4\_goals**, and **go/q4goals** will all take you to the same destination. Note that this means that if **go/q4-goals** already exists, you won’t be able to create **go/q4goals**, **go/q4-goals\_**, etc. A Go Link is editable by everyone by default. If needed, you can restrict edit access by checking **Restrict edit access only to me** under **More options**. After creating a Go Link, it will appear on the dashboard. **Learn how to create a Variable Go Link [here](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links)
.**

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#ways-to-create-go-links)

Ways to create Go Links
==============================================================================================================================

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#1-go-links-dashboard)

**1\. Go Links Dashboard**
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to [Tools > Go Links](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
 and click on the **New Go Link** button in the top right. ![Go Links Dashboard](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=fba6aec825a39948df108fd972b88007)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#2-glean-home-page)

**2\. Glean home page**
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a new Go Link via the **“New”** button in the top right. ![Glean Home Page](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=49cf39b6e865ea6ed6c5698aba9e2f47)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#3-search-result)

**3\. Search result**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also create a Go Link by clicking on the three-dot button that appears when hovering over a search result. ![Search Result Go Link](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=c34d95e103bb23b0b3ed72815da44a55)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#4-glean-sidebar)

**4\. Glean sidebar**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have the browser extension installed, create Go Links for the webpage you’re on. Open the sidebar using the shortcut **Command+J** for Mac and **Alt+J** for Windows. If the page already has a Go Link, you will see it there. ![Glean Sidebar](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=c4e843a211c6ac612b645699cad3afd9)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#5-error-page)

**5\. Error page**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you misspell a Go Link or type for a Go Link that doesn’t exist, you will land on an error page letting you know a link was not found. You’ll have the option to create a Go Link on that page. ![Error Page Go Link](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=83deb0755045d6b88c4cb36136393c94)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#using-go-links)

Using Go Links
============================================================================================================

**To use Go links, you must have the [Glean browser extension](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/glean/cfpdompphcacgpjfbonkdokgjhgabpij)
 installed or set up DNS-based redirection.** If using the extension, you must also **allow the extension to redirect Go Links**. If you have the extension installed, you’ll see a prompt to grant permissions at the top of [Tools > Go Links](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
. ![Go Links Permissions](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-7.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=fd365d2643a0f590256bdee1e3b25378) Simply type your Go Link in the browser URL bar (e.g. **go/onboarding**), and you’ll get automatically redirected to the corresponding URL. ![Go Link Redirection](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-8.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=6ff7f4993126d529f6e30d2dfb42d40c)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#sharing-go-links)

Sharing Go Links
================================================================================================================

Simply copy and paste a Go Link to share via email and Slack. You can also tell people verbally to go to **go/onboarding**. In Slack, the Glean slackbot will automatically unfurl Go Links in any public channel. ![Slack Go Links](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work-9.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=eb00b3b337c5971adac2c0e58347b119) If there is a Go Link(s) for a document, you’ll also see it reflected next to the document title on Glean search results.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#managing-go-links)

Managing Go Links
==================================================================================================================

*   Anyone in the organization can view all Go Links under [Tools > Go Links](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
    
*   Anyone in the organization can create a Go Link.
    *   If the user **selects** “Restrict edit access to only me”, only the creator, Go Link moderators, and admins should be able to edit the Go Link
    *   If the user **does not select** “Restrict edit access to only me”, every user should be able to edit the Go Link
*   Anyone in the organization can access a Go Link, while respecting document permissions in the native app.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work#usage-insights)

Usage insights
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have access to the Glean Insights, you can view the number of visits and unique visits by department from the dashboard.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/go-links/how-go-links-work)
.

YesNo

[How to make the most of Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links)
