[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#what-are-announcements%3F)

What are Announcements?
==========================================================================================================================================

Announcements are a great way to promote updates on Glean’s home page for your teammates to see, especially if many teammates are using [Glean as their new tab page](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/scio-search/cfpdompphcacgpjfbonkdokgjhgabpij)
. They can be targeted to a limited set of teammates for whatever duration you choose. ![Announcements Overview](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=70493271bae9e1227060ebb82d9710dd)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#create-an-announcement)

Create an Announcement
======================================================================================================================================

If you have permission to create Announcements for your team, navigate to [Knowledge > Announcements](https://app.askscio.com/knowledge/announcements)
 and click the **“New announcement”** button in the upper right corner. ![Navigate to Announcements](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=ea93e6cd99090291b40abd328e68bab4) You will see the announcement composer to create your announcement. ![Announcement Composer](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=2003baa654bfb8d84c26d110448975b9)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#customize-the-banner-area)

Customize the banner area
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose a background color, icon, or image. ![Banner Customization 1](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=e938956253218774827eca70f8a91dca) ![Banner Customization 2](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=c5c89feb8f05168578012808cc80402d) ![Banner Customization 3](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=ae95dfaad3a6b58615818ea47bc77e19) ![Banner Customization 4](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-7.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=489bd8b8c70d5b0dfe621b8f1d871479)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#write-your-announcement)

Write your announcement
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Give your announcement a title and use our WYSIWYG editor to easily compose your message. ![Writing Announcement](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-8.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=7e64b6fa8b196e2c387a78789473b99e)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#include-images)

Include images
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can include images to enhance your announcement. Please make sure that your image is less than 1MB in size. After placing your image, you can resize it by clicking it and then dragging the corner handle. ![Including Images](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-9.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=e950ece39cd4f8d253154b29f23b5331)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#include-a-video-url)

Include a video URL
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We currently support Youtube, Vimeo, and Google Drive links. ![Video URL](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/n_UlLNleo8r03xaq/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-10.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=n_UlLNleo8r03xaq&q=85&s=ab4fd33625b126474295c0ccb3919574) ![Video Integration](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-11.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=a4bdbe54b587ea824cb74c78f6252997)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#show-or-hide-the-announcement-author)

Show or hide the announcement author

If you prefer to hide the author name, turn off the _Show author_ toggle. ![Author Settings](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-12.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=44c839fe97852ffacb06a0eccfdbe41f) ![Author Visibility](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-13.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=0f4cd9873a967cd15867412a0a8cf41f)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#choose-your-audience)

Choose your audience

By default, your announcement will be shown to everyone in your organization. If you want to display the announcement to a select group of teammates, choose their _Department_ and _Location_. ![Audience Selection](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-14.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=1c347fbab5739bfbda8af7732b580123)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#schedule-when-it-should-appear-and-disappear-from-your-teammates%E2%80%99-home-pages)

Schedule when it should appear and disappear from your teammates’ home pages

By default, your announcement will be featured on your teammates’ home page for a month. You can change it by specifying the dates in _Scheduling_. ![Scheduling Announcements](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-15.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=5de4893aec8c49460e5d3f5856921693)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#preview-the-announcement)

Preview the announcement

Click on the _More_ button on the top right and select _Preview announcement_. ![Preview Option](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-16.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=3bfb3e8e6b5243b74bb41c74429a040e) ![Preview Announcement](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-17.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=9318975ea9c09c4fe66cd816a73deda8)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#publish-the-announcement)

Publish the announcement

Select the _Publish_ button, and your announcement will appear on your teammates’ home pages! ![Publish Announcement](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work-18.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=618351c4a3a521b1892b1d68b5a7d6f2)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#how-announcements-appear)

How Announcements appear
==========================================================================================================================================

If there are announcements visible to you, you’ll see an Announcements section on the Glean home page (or new tab page). You can click on the announcement itself to read in more detail, or hide it if irrelevant.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work#for-admins%3A)

==================================================================================================================

.

# Unlisted Go Links - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Go Links

Unlisted Go Links

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [How to create an Unlisted Go Link](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/unlisted-go-links#how-to-create-an-unlisted-go-link)
    

Unlisted Go Links are Go Links that are only visible to the creator of the Go Link and admins of Glean. Unlisted Go Links are great for private projects you don’t want others to accidentally discover.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/unlisted-go-links#how-to-create-an-unlisted-go-link)

How to create an Unlisted Go Link

![Create Unlisted Go Link](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/unlisted-go-links-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=14279067136e3f2f46e1fb4544252ff7)

*   Click on “**New Go Link**” on your [Go Links dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
     or on the Glean Home page
*   Fill out the form with a URL, name, and the description
*   Check “**Unlist**”

Your Go Link will no longer be discoverable on the Go Links dashboard by other users. A user who knows the Go Link and types it directly into the address bar can still access the Go Link. To make an unlisted Go Link discoverable to others again, simply uncheck the “**Unlist**.”

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/go-links/unlisted-go-links)
.

YesNo

[Create Variable Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links)

# How to use Team Pages - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Teams

How to use Team Pages

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Anatomy of a team page](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#anatomy-of-a-team-page)
    
*   [Team directory:](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#team-directory%3A)
    
*   [Teams in search:](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#teams-in-search%3A)
    

Glean’s team pages provide you and other employees at your company with a shared space to coordinate your efforts. Each page allows you to share what your team is working on, who’s on that team, and what the best way is to contact you. This way, it is easier for you to work within your team and share information across functions at your organization. At a minimum, Glean recommends creating team pages for all of your company’s departments, but the possibilities for what team pages you have are limitless! Customers use team pages to create workspaces for individual project pods, employee resource groups and social groups for particular geographic areas. Right now, only Glean admins and team moderators can create new team pages, so contact them for information on how to get new teams set up. This guide provides additional information on how to use team pages for teams you are a part of:

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#anatomy-of-a-team-page)

Anatomy of a team page
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Team profile pages contain detailed information about a team. Each page has a set of components, including:

*   Team name
*   What department the team is a part of
*   Team membersWho is on the teamWho leads the team
*   Team profile image
*   Banner image
*   “About” section for describing what the team does (this can include multiple paragraphs of rich text, with hyperlinks, images and more)
*   Contact infoEmail addresses to contact the team (can be a team alias, or any other address)Team Slack channelsURLs (can link to any page, including intranet and external content)

Glean recommends ensuring that your team pages have informative and up-to-date descriptions, and links to relevant contact information. Some ideas for information to put in your team’s description:

*   A description of what your team is responsible for
*   Information about who the correct contacts on your team are for cross-functional work
*   Links to project plans and quarterly goals
*   Information about upcoming events or key milestones

To edit these fields, click on the “edit” button in the upper-right-hand corner of the team page. Your organization may have particular style guides or best practices in place for teams pages — for information on that, contact your Glean admin.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#team-directory%3A)

Team directory:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For easy discoverability, teams appear in the directory alongside people. Teams can be sorted by relevance, team size, and alphabetically by name. Teams can also be filtered by name. The screenshot below is what part of the teams directory looks like when sorted by relevance for an engineer on the Verticals team that works closely with Product. Clicking on a team links to the team profile page.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages#teams-in-search%3A)

Teams in search:
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When your search indicates you are looking for a team, they will appear prominently in the results. These teams appear as expandable cards and can be expanded to show a subset of up to 6 members. Clicking on a card will take you to the team profile page. Teams will also show up as autocomplete results as you are typing a query. If you click on the team name, you will be taken to the team’s profile page.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Setting up Team Pages](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/setting-up-team-pages)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#discoverability)

Discoverability
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#go-links-extension-autocomplete)

Go Links extension autocomplete

With the Glean extension, teammates can search for Go Links directly from their URL bar. Type in **gl + space** to activate the Glean URL bar shortcut, then search for a Go Link. Below is an example of typing **gl + space**, then **go/product**. Glean’s autocomplete suggests Go Links matching **go/product**. ![Go Links Autocomplete](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=7d6b8342a976334c902be4b5e3cd959f)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#go-links-spellcheck)

Go Links spellcheck

When a teammate misspells a Go Link or wants to check if a certain Go Link already exists, Glean will show a page informing that the Go Link was not found. It will also suggest similar Go Links. Below is an example of typing **go/feedback**, then getting recommendations of similar Go Links. ![Go Links Spellcheck](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=3460ec1c0f83f7ea13067a6044284293)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#permissions)

Permissions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#view-and-edit-permissions)

View and edit permissions

Teammates can choose to [unlist their Go Link](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/unlisted-go-links)
 so it cannot be seen by other teammates as well as restrict edit access to only themselves. Go Links moderators and admins are still able to edit Go Links with restricted edit access.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#go-links-moderator-role)

Go Links moderator role

Admins can set certain teammates as Go Links moderators. As a moderator, they can edit Go Links, even those that have been set to be non-editable by their creators. This is useful in cases where a Go Link needs to be updated or corrected, but the original creator is not available or has left the organization Watch how to set teammate permissions on the [Admin Guide: Teammates Tab](https://docs.glean.com/administration/identity/roles/manage-users)
 page.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links#go-links-dashboard)

Go Links Dashboard

Create and manage all Go Links from the dashboard which can be found under “Tools.” Filter Go Links by creator, department, and Go Link type (Unlisted, Public, Variable). ![Go Links Dashboard](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=49b6a5869f8e413d2a34d87b0cf91c51)

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/go-links/how-to-make-the-most-of-go-links)
.

# Troubleshooting Go Links - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

⌘K

Go Links

Troubleshooting Go Links

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)

[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [If you are seeing an error saying “This site can’t be reached”](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting#if-you-are-seeing-an-error-saying-%E2%80%9Cthis-site-can%E2%80%99t-be-reached%E2%80%9D)
    
*   [If you are seeing a page that says “Oops, no Go Link here!”](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting#if-you-are-seeing-a-page-that-says-%E2%80%9Coops%2C-no-go-link-here-%E2%80%9D)
    

If you’re having trouble accessing a [Go Link](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work)
, this guide will walk you through potential solutions to that problem.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting#if-you-are-seeing-an-error-saying-%E2%80%9Cthis-site-can%E2%80%99t-be-reached%E2%80%9D)

If you are seeing an error saying “This site can’t be reached”
==================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Check to make sure you have the Glean Browser Extension installed and enabled. Go Links require the latest version of the extension to function. In Chrome, go to [chrome://extensions](chrome://extensions)
, and look for Glean. If it’s not there, download the extension from the Chrome Web Store. ![The Glean extension in Chrome, with a toggle showing that it is enabled](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting-go-links-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=b19ecff8e81f4aeea86adaff547939bd) If it is there, make sure that it’s enabled: the toggle in the lower right corner should be switched on and over to the right. After that, quit and reopen Chrome, and try accessing the Go Link again. If that still doesn’t work, go to the [Go Links directory](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
. You may need to enable additional permissions from the banner at the top of the directory to make Go Links function in your browser.

* * *

![Screenshot of text showing "Oops, no Go Link here" taken from the Go Links error page](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting-go-links-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=86c483632e860db9feaf049193d7a48d)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting#if-you-are-seeing-a-page-that-says-%E2%80%9Coops%2C-no-go-link-here-%E2%80%9D)

If you are seeing a page that says “Oops, no Go Link here!”
======================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Check to make sure you typed the Go Link correctly. If you have typed it correctly, it’s possible that you were accidentally given the wrong Go Link. You can search Glean for the correct resource, or filter the [Go Links Directory](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
 for your organization to find it. If someone else gave you the Go Link, check with them to make sure they sent you the right one.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/troubleshooting/troubleshooting-go-links)
.

# Updating Permissions On Collections - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Collections

Updating Permissions On Collections

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Who Can Change Permissions](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#who-can-change-permissions)
    
*   [How to Change Permissions](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#how-to-change-permissions)
    
*   [How Permissions on Child Collections Work](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#how-permissions-on-child-collections-work)
    

Collections are an easy way to organize related documents across all your tools and any URL from the web by a single topic. When you want to use Collections as a source of truth on a particular topic, you may want to restrict which teammates can edit contents of that Collection. Here’s how you can control who has edit access over a single Collection.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#who-can-change-permissions)

Who Can Change Permissions
=========================================================================================================================================================

1.  **Owners:** Owners can add or remove other owners and editors, ensuring that the right people have the appropriate level of access.
    *   The creator of a collection is automatically assigned as the Owner and has the ability to manage permissions.
    *   The company’s overall Collection Moderator has Owner rights to all Collections by default.
2.  **Editors:** Editors can add or remove other editors from the Collection

**Note:** All Collections will always be viewable by the entire company. You can restrict any individual from viewing a specific Collection.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#how-to-change-permissions)

How to Change Permissions
=======================================================================================================================================================

If you’re the an owner or editor of a Collection

1.  **Open the Collection**: Navigate to the collection for which you want to change permissions.
2.  **Click the Share Button**: Locate and click the Share button on the collection page. ![Share Button](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=5a34eb2e2acf439a4061b0df28e07324)
3.  **Manage Permissions**: In the sharing settings, you can:
    
    *   Add individual owners and editors.
    *   Change the permission level of the entire company from editors to viewers.
    *   Remove access for specific users or departments.
    
    ![Manage Permissions](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=fa7e502392bd8a03bd59ae96225ac787)
4.  New permissions are auto-saved. Click ‘Done’ to exit.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections#how-permissions-on-child-collections-work)

How Permissions on Child Collections Work
=======================================================================================================================================================================================

Child Collections (Collections created under a top parent Collection) automatically inherit the permissions of their parent Collection. This means:

*   **Inherited Permissions**: Any permissions set on the parent Collection will apply to the child Collection.
*   **Adding Permissions**: Owners and editors of the child Collection can add new editors or owners to the child collection.
*   **Non-Removable Inherited Permissions**: Inherited permissions cannot be removed from the child collection.

![Child Collection Permissions](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=63330dc1caf25264f18a03094bf5a95c)

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[How Go Links Work](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/how-go-links-work)

# Shortcuts - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Home Page

Shortcuts

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [What Are Shortcuts in Profile Settings?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#what-are-shortcuts-in-profile-settings%3F)
    
*   [How to Enable Shortcuts in Your Profile Settings](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#how-to-enable-shortcuts-in-your-profile-settings)
    
*   [Managing Your Shortcuts](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#managing-your-shortcuts)
    
*   [Adding ‘My Shortcuts’](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#adding-%E2%80%98my-shortcuts%E2%80%99)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#what-are-shortcuts-in-profile-settings%3F)

What Are Shortcuts in Profile Settings?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Shortcuts in profile settings are quick links to websites or pages you visit frequently. They provide easy and fast access to these sites directly from your home page, saving you time and helping you stay organized.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#how-to-enable-shortcuts-in-your-profile-settings)

How to Enable Shortcuts in Your Profile Settings
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow these simple steps to enable shortcuts and start managing them in your profile settings:

1.  Access ‘Your Settings’
    *   Navigate to your profile settings by clicking on your profile icon.
2.  Enable Shortcuts
    *   Under **Preferences**, go to the **General** section. Find the option labeled **Show Shortcuts** and toggle it On. This will enable the shortcut feature. ![images](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/pF_0vASXWAL79iHb/images/shortcuts1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=pF_0vASXWAL79iHb&q=85&s=cd8e6bb9face27de0056562fe75cb482)                            

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#managing-your-shortcuts)

Managing Your Shortcuts
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the feature is enabled, managing your shortcuts is easy. Here’s how:

1.  Navigate to the Glean Home Page
    *   Go to the Glean home page, where you’ll now notice a small menu with three dots (…). This is the **Manage Shortcuts** option. ![images](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/pF_0vASXWAL79iHb/images/shortcuts2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=pF_0vASXWAL79iHb&q=85&s=dfadb058ee7d33d392c8fbbf00af8951)                          
2.  Click on these three dots i.e ‘Manage Shortcuts’
    *   When you click on **Manage Shortcuts**, you’ll be presented with two options:
    *   **Top Sites**: This section automatically displays sites you visit most frequently. If enabled, these sites will appear on your home page for quick access.
    *   **My Shortcuts**: Clicking this option will reveal the ‘Add Shortcut’ sub-tab, which will now be highlighted (previously dimmed). This is where you can manually add and customize the sites you want to appear as your preferred shortcuts. ![images](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/pF_0vASXWAL79iHb/images/shortcuts3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=pF_0vASXWAL79iHb&q=85&s=098b1cfcb7ade08e26e2e6f4132716fd)                               

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/home-page/shortcuts#adding-%E2%80%98my-shortcuts%E2%80%99)

Adding ‘My Shortcuts’
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add a new shortcut, follow these simple steps:

1.  Click on the ‘Add Shortcut’ option in the My Shortcuts tab.
2.  A small dialog box will appear asking for the name and URL of the site you want to add. Enter this information and click Add.
3.  Once the shortcut is created, you will receive a confirmation message on the screen. The icon for the site will also appear in your home page’s Shortcuts section.

While both Shortcuts and Go Links serve the purpose of providing quick access, they are distinct features. Shortcuts are designed for personal use, offering quick links to frequently visited sites. In contrast, Go Links are a specialized feature within Glean, intended for creating easy-to-remember URLs for company resources. This makes it easier to navigate internal tools and resources.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[How Announcements Work](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/announcements/how-announcements-work)

# Create Variable Go Links - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Go Links

Create Variable Go Links

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [How to create a Variable Go Link](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links#how-to-create-a-variable-go-link)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links#examples)
    

Variable Go Links redirect to specific destinations when a custom value like a ticket # are added, powering hundreds of pages within a website. Users can make any part of an URL variable with a denotation and append Go Link URL to target specific destinations such as search results page or support tickets.

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links#how-to-create-a-variable-go-link)

How to create a Variable Go Link

1.  Click on “New Go Link” on your [Go Links dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/golinks)
     or Glean Home Page.
2.  Fill in the Destination URL and identify the part of the URL (parameter) to make variable and replace it with **`{*}`.** You will see “**Variable**” pop up when it detects a\*\*`{*}`\*\*.

*   Example: **`glean.atlassian.net/123`** -> **`glean.atlassian.net/{*}`**

3.  Fill in “Default Go Link to”. This is to specify the default destination URL for the Go Link without a variable.

*   Example: You can specify **go/jira** to be redirected to **glean.atlassian.net**

Note: When typing a variable Go Link, the substitution would be denoted by another “/” following go/jira (E.g. **go/jira/123**). There can be multiple variable substitutions in a single URL (E.g. **go/jira/123/abc**) ![Create Variable Go Link](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=270efd4b3148c6e26ca22e4a8eee88cd)

### 

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/create-variable-go-links#examples)

Examples

Use Variable Go Links to quickly navigate to search result pages

*   `https://app.glean.com/search?q={*}` -> `https://app.glean.com/search?q=expense-policy`
*   `https://github.com/search?q={*}` -> `https://github.com/search?q=fastapi`

\*Note that Variable Go Links support spaces (E.g. you can search for “how do go links work” using “_go/glean/how do go links work”_ Use Variable Go Links to quickly navigate to specific issues and tickets

*   `https://app.atlassian.net/browse/PROD-{*}` -> `https://app.atlassian.net/browse/PROD-79845`
*   `https://github.com/product/{*}/issues/{*}` -> `https://github.com/product/featureX/issues/BUG-1234`

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/go-links/create-variable-go-links)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Troubleshooting Go Links](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/go-links/troubleshooting)

# How Collections Work - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Collections

How Collections Work

[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [What are Collections?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#what-are-collections%3F)

![Collections Overview](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=10dc0f03ac908eb49819fdef271eb288)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#what-are-collections%3F)

What are Collections?
==================================================================================================================================

Collections are an easy way to organize related documents across all your tools by a single topic. You can think of them as a way to curate a set of documents for other teammates to find and use easily. **Have a big launch coming up?** Group that planning doc, Jira epic, design folder, and marketing communications in a single collection, so your cross-functional team stays aligned. **Have someone new joining your team?** Organize all the onboarding information that a new employee needs to get up and running into a collection, and share the link with them on their first day. **Have documents related to a horizontal or vertical scattered everywhere?** Group those docs into a collection so your teammates can find what they need quickly. The use cases are endless! Let’s take a look at how collections work.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#create-a-collection)

Create a Collection
============================================================================================================================

Open the [Collections dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/collections)
, and click “New Collection” in the upper right-hand corner. Then create the collection’s title (choose something that will describe its contents), select an emoji to be used as the collection’s icon and then enter a description. Don’t worry if you don’t have the perfect idea for these yet! You can change them any time.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#add-items-to-a-collection)

Add items to a Collection
========================================================================================================================================

![Adding Items to Collections](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=7b1201be38a77a0f6efac7a44c5839dd)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#from-the-collection-page)

From the collection page
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add links to a collection by clicking on one of the five options in the ”+ Add ” drop-down menu seen above. Clicking “Document” will pull up a search box that allows you to look for any files you want that Glean indexes. Click on the “Add to Collection” button next to a search result to add it to the collection. From this view, you can add multiple items to a collection at once: keep searching and adding until you’ve found everything you want to include. (There is no technical limit on the number of items in a collection, but we recommend keeping them to no more than 30 items for readability purposes.) You can also add content you can’t find searching Glean by using the “🌐URL” option in that same drop-down menu. This helps organize content like external media mentions or sites that don’t make sense to include in Glean’s index, like an expense reporting system or benefits portal. When added via search, Glean will automatically populate the item’s title, offer an integrated preview on the collection page, and show that the item is tagged in a collection on search results so users can easily find related information. Items added to a collection via URL will only show a link and will not include the integrated preview or search result tags.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#from-the-search-results-page)

**From the search results page**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Search to pull up the document(s) you want to add to your collection. Hover over the document, click on the three dot menu, and use the “**Add to Collection**” quick action from the results. ![Search Results Add to Collection](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=a2ef602326c2bd6a99323bb54588a723) You can add Answers and documents from connected workplace apps to Collections. In the modal that appears, you can quickly filter to add the document to a Collection that already exists or create a new one.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#add-descriptions-to-collection-items)

Add descriptions to collection items
==============================================================================================================================================================

Once an item is in a collection, you can give it a brief, one-paragraph description, so other people viewing the collection can understand its purpose and why it has been included. For example, if you’ve created an onboarding collection for your team, use these description fields to help guide people through the onboarding process, provide instructions about setting up their GitHub profile, or fill out a form to request office supplies.

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#see-collections-in-search-results)

See Collections in search results
========================================================================================================================================================

When a document is part of a Collection, you’ll see the Collection on the search result. ![Collections in Search Results](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=6e5f82dd853b231f85e777e599c6dec1) You can also filter by Collection using the filters under the search box or use the search operator `app:collections`

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#view-all-collections-across-your-company)

View all collections across your company
======================================================================================================================================================================

You can view all of your company’s collections from the Collections dashboard, which can be [found here](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/collections/)
. From this dashboard, you can create new collections, search for collections other people have created using the “Filter” box directly above the gallery table, and delete collections. Deleting a Collection won’t delete or affect any of the underlying documents within it - it will just remove the Collection from Glean. ![Collections Dashboard](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=2a5ca12c421f29162e8912bf9ac15318)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#organize-collections)

Organize Collections
==============================================================================================================================

You can organize Collections into sections using [Headers](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers)
 or create [Subcollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections)
 to nest collections within. ![Organizing Collections](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=0e6068b694c395f0bdf631758fc215dc)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#edit-sharing-permissions-on-collections)

Edit sharing permissions on Collections
====================================================================================================================================================================

You can update permissions for which teammates or departments should have edit access to the contents of any collection using the Share button. ![Sharing Permissions](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work-7.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=4e7463eacf0ac707c78ae5d8174b62ed)

* * *

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work#questions%3F-feature-requests%3F)

Questions? Feature requests?
==================================================================================================================================================

Get in touch with us via the Messenger 👉

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/collections/how-collections-work)
.

# Organizing Collections Using Headers - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Collections

Organizing Collections Using Headers

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [What are Headers?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers#what-are-headers%3F)
    
*   [How to create Headers](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers#how-to-create-headers)
    

Collections are an easy way to organize related documents across all your tools and any URL from the web by a single topic. As teams start creating Collections with more than a few items, it can become harder for people to navigate and find the most relevant or important item within the Collection. Here’s how you can use Headers to better organize.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers#what-are-headers%3F)

What are Headers?
==========================================================================================================================================

Headers are used to label different sections within a Collection to provide more context on a group of documents. For example, you can use headers to:

*   Group documents by order of importance using “Start here” “Must reads”
*   Group documents by different projects
*   Group documents by topics such as “Onboarding” “Technical resources” “Project backgrounds”

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers#how-to-create-headers)

How to create Headers
================================================================================================================================================

You can create headers the same way you add any documents and links by clicking on the **\+ Add** button on the top right corner of the Collection. You can also insert Headers between existing documents or add Headers to the bottom of the page by clicking the **+---** button from the place you want to add headers to. ![Organizing Collections Using Headers](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=482a24cbfc6c173e4e0a0a67a7c568da) If you are looking for ways to organize by creating hierarchy of information, you can use [Subcollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers)
 to create Collections within a Collection.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/collections/organizing-collections-using-headers)
.

Was this page helpful?

[Providing Informational Hierarchy Using Subcollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections)

# Providing Informational Hierarchy Using Subcollections - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Collections

Providing Informational Hierarchy Using Subcollections

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [What are SubCollections?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#what-are-subcollections%3F)
    
*   [How to create SubCollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#how-to-create-subcollections)
    
*   [Moving SubCollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#moving-subcollections)
    
*   [Accessing Subcollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#accessing-subcollections)
    
*   [Number of Subcollections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#number-of-subcollections)
    

[Collections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/how-collections-work)
 are an easy way to organize related documents across all your tools and any URL from the web by a single topic. As teams start creating Collections with more than a few items, it can become harder for people to navigate and find the most relevant or important item within the Collection. Here’s how you can use Subcollections to better organize.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#what-are-subcollections%3F)

What are SubCollections?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SubCollections are nested collections under a main collection, providing ways to build a more robust collection with a large number of items. It prevents a single collection from being too long to navigate even with Headers, while also providing informational hierarchy. For example, you can create a subcollection for:

*   Subteams, subtopics, or subprojects under the main Collection for a team or topic. For example, creating a subcollection for a product feature within a Collection for a product team
*   When there are different audiences under the same umbrella topics. i.e. creating a subcollection for BDR and AE under “Onboarding” header/topic
*   When you have more than 5 items (documents and links) under the same topic, making it too long to be organized under a Header
    *   We also encourage organizing using subcollection when the main collection becomes a list of 20+ documents and links.

See a demo of Subcollections [here](https://www.loom.com/share/5969473e092d4779b5655bae5fa181f2)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#how-to-create-subcollections)

How to create SubCollections
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can create a Subcollection the same way you add any documents and links to a collection by clicking ”+ Add New Collection” button on the top right corner of the Collection. You can also insert Subcollection between existing documents or add to the bottom of the page by clicking the **+---** button from the place you want to add a Subcollection to. ![SubCollections Creation](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=99c9b27adcee1626bbcdb405dfb698b3)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#moving-subcollections)

Moving SubCollections
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Collections can be nested under other Collections by clicking on the 3-dot menu on the Collections dashboard and selecting “Move” and moving the Collection to an appropriate parent Collection. Please note that there can only be one parent Collection for every Subcollection. ![Moving SubCollections](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU/images/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uSHOVvwKjGVdBPeU&q=85&s=211711727af76b291bdd9f6a34d7abb2)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#accessing-subcollections)

Accessing Subcollections
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   See SubCollections in search results
    *   Subcollection will appear on the search results based on relevancy
    *   When a document is part of a SubCollection, you’ll see the SubCollection on the search result
*   SubCollection will not appear on the main Collections dashboard in order to help organization of the dashboard

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections#number-of-subcollections)

Number of Subcollections
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can create up to 20 Collections within a collection and up to 2 sublevels (Main Collection -> sub collections -> collection within a sub collection) for a 3 layer of Collections hierarchy

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/collections/providing-informational-hierarchy-using-subcollections)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Updating Permissions On Collections](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/collections/updating-permissions-on-collections)

# What Should I Do With Documents That Are Completely Out Of Date? - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Document Verification

What Should I Do With Documents That Are Completely Out Of Date?

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Unsharing a document](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#unsharing-a-document)
    
*   [Deprecating a document](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#deprecating-a-document)
    
*   [How to deprecate a document](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#how-to-deprecate-a-document)
    
*   [What happens after I’ve deprecated a document?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#what-happens-after-i%E2%80%99ve-deprecated-a-document%3F)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#unsharing-a-document)

Unsharing a document
==========================================================================================================================================================================

We get it. Sometimes, documents are just completely out of date and it’s best to remove them entirely. If you have such a document that is still being viewed by your teammates, then there are a few actions to take. If the document is not valuable at all anymore, it’s best to **unshare it or delete it** so that no one else will stumble across it. You will need to navigate to the document itself to **manually unshare or delete the document.** Glean does not have write permissions so you won’t be able to unshare or delete the document from Glean itself.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#deprecating-a-document)

Deprecating a document
==============================================================================================================================================================================

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#how-to-deprecate-a-document)

How to deprecate a document
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your document is no longer valid but may still have some value, you can mark it as **Deprecated** to act as a warning to your teammates. This is similar to modifying the title of your document to include the words “deprecated”. For example, there might be documentation for an old product design that’s no longer in production, but can serve as a helpful reference for discussions or ideation in the future. To deprecate a document, go to the **Verification > Your content** and click on the **Deprecate** button for a document. You’ll see a confirmation in a modal, and also get an option to unshare the document itself. ![Deprecation Modal](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=10ae890501d16b0e90619f77fd4c45d6)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date#what-happens-after-i%E2%80%99ve-deprecated-a-document%3F)

What happens after I’ve deprecated a document?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Deprecated documents may still appear on Glean search results. However, a deprecated symbol will appear next to the document on the search results page. This status will also be seen from the document itself. ![Deprecated Document in Search Results](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=c3a1fd5dbcb1b46e126c0ca357e8b361)

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/verifying-documents/what-should-i-do-with-documents-that-are-completely-out-of-date)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[How to use Team Pages](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/people/teams/how-to-use-team-pages)

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Pins

How Pins Work

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)

On this page

*   [What are Pins?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#what-are-pins%3F)

![Pins Overview](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=e1356d2dd07fd4ad1c66c86ff330221b)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#what-are-pins%3F)

What are Pins?
======================================================================================================

Pins are results that always appear at the top of a search results page for a query and audience that you choose. Public pins appear for you and other users at your company, while private pins are only visible to you.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#create-a-pin)

Create a Pin
================================================================================================

You can create a pin from the search results page or the [pin dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/pins)
 in Glean’s knowledge tab.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#create-a-pin-from-a-search-results-page)

Create a Pin from a search results page
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From the search results page for a query, hover over the result you would like to pin and click on the pushpin icon. ![Create Pin from Search](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=e81310f3ede2546e98c41dbeab813b5b)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#create-a-pin-from-the-pins-dashboard)

Create a Pin from the Pins dashboard
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Navigate to [Knowledge > Pins](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/pins)
. Click the New Pin button, and you’ll be prompted to search for and select the resource you would like to pin. ![Pins Dashboard](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=b516f192db8d1dcc5bf9f7c7a61e7443) You can input additional queries for your Pin by clicking Add a query.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#choose-an-audience-for-your-pin)

**Choose an audience for your Pin**
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you’ve selected the result to pin, you’ll be able to specify the audience it shows up for. ![Pin Audience Selection](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=3f265f7d1008d8ec50fcf01df3a1ba8e)

*   Selecting “Only Me” will create a private pin that will only appear at the top of search results for you and nobody else.
*   Selecting “Teammates” will create a public pin that appears for other users within your company. The audience dropdown allows you to choose which departments at your company see the pin; leaving it blank will have the pin appear for everyone at your organization.

If you don’t see “Teammates” as an option, your organization’s Glean admin has locked public pin creation. Contact them to get access.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#view-pins-in-search-results)

View Pins in search results
==============================================================================================================================

If a Pin is visible to you for your query, you’ll see it at the top of the search results. Each pin will have the name of the person who pinned the result, as well as the person who last edited it. Private pins will show that they are only visible to you. Glean respects all source permissions for pinned items, so users will only see pins in search results when they have access to the underlying item.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#view-pins-across-your-company)

View Pins across your company
==================================================================================================================================

You can see all pins that you are in the audience for in the [pins dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/pins)
, including public and private pins. Admins and users with the pin moderator role will be able to see all public pins across the company as well.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/pins/how-pins-work#removing-a-pin)

Removing a Pin
====================================================================================================

To remove a Pin, click the more menu on the right hand side of the Pin on the [Pins dashboard](https://app.glean.com/knowledge/pins)
, and select “Delete Pin”. This button may be disabled depending on the permissions set for Pins by your Glean admin.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/pins/how-pins-work)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[How Verification Works](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# What Does Verification Mean? - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Document Verification

What Does Verification Mean?

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)

[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [For example](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-does-verification-mean#for-example)
    

**Verification** is your stamp of approval on the accuracy of a document you own. By letting your teammates know your document is verified to be accurate, they can use the information in their work with confidence.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/what-does-verification-mean#for-example)

For example
====================================================================================================================

An engineer can **verify a tech plan**, so other engineers from different teams can input on the latest decisions with any dependencies or considerations. A product manager can **verify the release notes of a feature**, so Sales and Support teams can use that information in conversations with prospective and current customers. A designer can **verify a design proposal**, so engineers know it contains the most up-to-date requirements and designs for a feature they’re building. And many more! Get in touch via the Messenger with any questions or share use cases of your own.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/verifying-documents/what-does-verification-mean)
