# Which Documents Should I Verify? - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

Ctrl K

Search...

Navigation

Document Verification

Which Documents Should I Verify?

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)
[Security & Architecture](https://docs.glean.com/security/home)
[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [Which documents should I verify?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/which-documents-should-i-verify#which-documents-should-i-verify%3F)
    
*   [Respond to verification requests](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/which-documents-should-i-verify#respond-to-verification-requests)
    

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/which-documents-should-i-verify#which-documents-should-i-verify%3F)

Which documents should I verify?
====================================================================================================================================================================

A few good questions to ask yourself on any document is:

*   Will someone from another department look at this document for information they need?
*   Will this information be used by Sales or Marketing to create customer material?
*   Will someone on my team waste time if they use this information and it’s no longer accurate? Requirements docs, design docs, FAQs, wiki pages, and debugging instructions are good examples.

If you answer **Yes** to any of these questions, it’s probably a good document to **Verify** and focus on keeping up to date. _Note: this is not a comprehensive guide and you’ll have to use your own intuition on how valuable a document is._ **For example…** An engineer can **verify a tech plan,** so other engineers from different teams can input on the latest decisions with any dependencies or considerations. A product manager can **verify the release notes of a feature**, so Sales and Support teams can use that information in conversations with prospective and current customers. A designer can **verify a design proposal,** so engineers know it contains the most up-to-date requirements and designs for a feature they’re building.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/which-documents-should-i-verify#respond-to-verification-requests)

Respond to verification requests
==================================================================================================================================================================

When other teammates **request verification** on a document you own, or if it’s time to re-verify documents based on your own reminders, those documents appear on **Verification > Your tasks.** You can verify or deprecate documents from the list. ![Verification Tasks](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/which-documents-should-i-verify-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=6128bf08865dfdb9e2f655eb5b9de09f)

* * *

Questions? Let us know in the Messenger.

Looking for the original version of this page? You can find the archived version [here](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/verifying-documents/which-documents-should-i-verify)
.

# How Verification Works - Glean Help Center

[Glean Help Center home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=828d510ca943686b81ff369fb06b7ed0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a1901d91185c53325fe9ba60d993b592)](https://docs.glean.com/)

Search...

Ctrl K

Search...

Navigation

Document Verification

How Verification Works

[Home](https://docs.glean.com/home)
[User Guide](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/about/what-is-glean)
[Agents](https://docs.glean.com/agents/home)
[Protect](https://docs.glean.com/protect/ai-security/home)
[Get Started for Admins](https://docs.glean.com/get-started/welcome)
[Connectors](https://docs.glean.com/connectors/home)
[Admin Guide](https://docs.glean.com/administration/about)

[Troubleshooting](https://docs.glean.com/troubleshooting/home)
[Release Notes](https://docs.glean.com/release-notes/home)
[Archive](https://docs.glean.com/archive/help-glean/getting-started-in-glean/what-is-glean)

On this page

*   [See verified search results](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#see-verified-search-results)
    
*   [Track what documents need your verification](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#track-what-documents-need-your-verification)
    
*   [Verification tasks](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verification-tasks)
    
*   [Your content](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#your-content)
    
*   [Verifying a document](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-a-document)
    
*   [Verifying from the web app](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-web-app)
    
*   [Ask for verification on your teammates’ documents](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#ask-for-verification-on-your-teammates%E2%80%99-documents)
    
*   [Verifying from the web app](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-web-app-2)
    
*   [Verifying from the Chrome extension](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-chrome-extension)
    
*   [Questions or feedback?](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#questions-or-feedback%3F)
    

When you’re using Glean to search for documents across different tools in your company, Glean’s Verification feature makes it easy to know if a document is **verified**: personally approved by one of your teammates that it’s accurate and up to date. You can also track which of your documents your teammates want you to verify and set proactive reminders to help you keep your documents up to date.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#see-verified-search-results)

See verified search results
===============================================================================================================================================

A **verified search result** appears with a **green badge** after a result title. Hover over the badge to see who verified the document and when. This way, before you even click on a document, you can check if it’s up to date or not. ![Verified Search Results](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=cd1bb3bdcbf06dcb403c5b44d16015d6)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#track-what-documents-need-your-verification)

Track what documents need your verification
===============================================================================================================================================================================

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verification-tasks)

Verification tasks
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **[Knowledge > Verification > Tasks](http://app.glean.com/verification)
** you can see which documents your teammates have requested your verification on, as well as your own reminders to re-verify documents to keep them updated. ![Verification Tasks](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=12a57e2b9aeb2bd94b39a16dae36a047)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#your-content)

Your content
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also go to **[Knowledge > Verification > Your Content](https://app.glean.com/verification/content)
** to see all the content you own across various apps, and use the filters at the top of the page to drill into what’s unverified, verified, and deprecated. Verify and deprecate documents from there to help your teammates work from the most up-to-date content. ![Your Content](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=cb8c1a44d9c70b7689be4511ef79d7ec)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-a-document)

Verifying a document
=================================================================================================================================

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-web-app)

Verifying from the web app
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verify a document via your [Tasks](http://app.glean.com/verification)
 list. After verifying, set a reminder to reverify the document to ensure that your content stays fresh. When the reminder is up, you’ll see this document pop back into your Tasks list. ![Verifying Document](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=3c6f70c53c9ed06df388b068af34b7b1)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#ask-for-verification-on-your-teammates%E2%80%99-documents)

Ask for verification on your teammates’ documents
===================================================================================================================================================================================================

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-web-app-2)

Verifying from the web app
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hover over a search result and under the “more” menu (three dots), click “Request verification”. You’ll be able to select a verification reason as well to provide more details. ![Request Verification](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=3a06831c2fbe3c791527a8abf87a2697)

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#verifying-from-the-chrome-extension)

Verifying from the Chrome extension
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you visit a teammate’s document (if you have the Chrome extension enabled), you can see whether the doc is verified, unverified, or deprecated in the Glean sticky tabs on the bottom right. ![Chrome Extension Verification](https://mintcdn.com/glean-5786559b/oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp/images/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oQFXWQsCPyCQbpvp&q=85&s=a84eb6274e844234f2ad75eb71c4712c) Click on the tab and you can see more details about the verification status and request verification from the teammate.

[​](https://docs.glean.com/user-guide/knowledge/verification/how-verification-works#questions-or-feedback%3F)

Questions or feedback?
=======================================================================================================================================

Chat with us in the Messenger! 🙌
